This Week

— Special Dispatch from Beiping

—Changes in Personnel of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council—

General observations: The Japanese side's pressure on the Hebei-Chahar authorities has seemingly eased recently compared to before. However, under the threat of their large garrison, their long-advocated "economic cooperation" and various other piecemeal demands have not been paused slightly and are urgently seeking to be put into practice first. However, the current difficulty in implementing them is the issue of selecting responsible individuals. Therefore, partial changes and supplements to the Hebei-Chahar political authorities are inevitable. The following is a record of the personnel involved:

Li Sihao: Negotiations for Li's appointment as Chairman of the Economic Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council were underway even before Wang Kemin. Wang could not take office due to numerous obstacles, so Li was invited to take the position, thus reviving his career. Li finally flew from Shanghai to Beiping on the 10th of this month. By then, negotiations had matured, so all relevant parties were unwilling to express their opinions. Some even thought Li's visit north was to inspect the business of the Da Zhong Bank, which he had been operating, and that he would soon return to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, the situation took a sudden turn, and Li's appointment as Chairman of the Economic Committee was officially announced and scheduled to take office within two or three days. On the morning of the 15th, he formally took office at the council. On the afternoon of the 18th, he went to Tianjin, staying there for two days. During this time, he held separate discussions with Tashiro, senior staff of the Japanese garrison, and Horiuchi Kanjo, the Japanese Consul-General in Tianjin. Li held important financial positions in the Beiyang government era. In the 13th year of the Republic (1924), when Duan Qirui was in power, Li was a key figure in the controversial Nishihara Loans. Until recently, he still held considerable influence in finance and was an old friend of Tashiro and Horiuchi of the Japanese side.

Lu Zongyu: Held several prominent positions in the Beiyang government era. In the 8th year of the Republic (1919), the "May Fourth" Movement was triggered by his negotiations with Japan. Lu, along with Cao Rulin and Zhang Zongxiang, was criticized by the Chinese people. In recent years, he has been living in seclusion in Tianjin. Since the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, there have been several rumors of him taking up a certain position, but these have never materialized. In recent years, Lu has repeatedly voiced his grievances, believing that foreigners misunderstood him regarding the events of the 8th year of the Republic, leaving him unable to defend himself. Therefore, his current emergence may be a rare opportunity to make amends. Various parties here are paying close attention to Lu's future actions.

Qi Xieyuan: Qi went into seclusion in Tianjin after stepping down as Military Governor of Jiangsu. Since the North China Incident occurred last July, Qi has been one of the many retired officials active in Tianjin. After the Hebei-Chahar Political Council appointed Qi as a member, the relationship between Qi and the Hebei-Chahar authorities slightly changed. The original plan for this personnel change in the Hebei-Chahar situation was to establish a standing committee of five members in the political council, with Qi, Jia Deyao, Cao Rulin, Qin Dechun, and Zhang Zizhong serving as members. Later, Cao expressed his unwillingness to take office, so the plan was changed, with Qi, Jia, and Qin serving as "Standing Committee Members Attending Office Regularly" to assist Song in handling everything.

Shi Yousan: Shi Yousan and Song Zheyuan and other figures from the 19th Route Army were originally comrades in the former Northwest Army. Later, as the situation changed, they each pursued their own paths, with Shi's changes being particularly numerous. During the Tianjin Incident in the 20th year of the Republic (1931) and the Bai Jianwu rebellion in Fengtai last year, people blamed Shi. In fact, Shi's activities have not stopped since the September 18th Incident (Mukden Incident). The arrest warrant had long been posted at the national borders. This spring, the Hebei-Chahar authorities, in view of various circumstances and facts, simultaneously revoked the arrest warrants for Shi, Hao Peng, and Bai Jianwu. After that, the relationship between Shi and the Hebei-Chahar authorities underwent a major change. Until recently, there have been many rumors in society about Shi, Qi Xieyuan, and others being active in Tianjin. Therefore, on the 18th of this month, the authorities here announced that Shi was appointed as the Commander of the Hebei Northern Border Area Security, although the area under his jurisdiction is not large, it also expresses the authorities' intention to rely on him. Whether the reputation of Shi, Qi, and others can be salvaged by this opportunity will depend on their future actions.

Zhang Shizhao: Zhang held important positions such as Minister of Education in the Beiyang government era. When the issue of the Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Economic Committee was shelved after Wang Kemin, Li Sihao, Zhang Hu, and others were considered, there was talk of inviting Zhang to take the position. Now that the position of Chairman of the Economic Committee has been filled by Li Sihao, Zhang has also taken office as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and has further succeeded Deng Zhexi as Chairman of the Legal System Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council.

Page 5

Current Commentary

Reassessing British Far East Policy

— Fortunately

In the current state of China's foreign relations, Britain exerts a significant influence. Britain's policy of protecting Far Eastern markets, and indeed all its economic and political activities on the world stage, seem to be closely related to China's destiny.

Everyone knows that the keynote of British Far East policy had already seen some significant manifestations during Sir Frederick Leith-Ross's visit to China last year. After he returned to London, Britain became even more active in the Far East. Leaving aside Britain's investment activities in the Yangtze River and South China over the years, let's just talk about the events of the past few months. Rogers, the famous British monetary expert who accompanied Leith-Ross to China last year, has returned to China, reportedly to continue Sir Ross's mission. Recently, the British Export Credits Guarantee Department dispatched Conservative MP Mr. Patrick as the department's representative in China. We can understand the significance of this matter at a glance. As for the rumored £10 million loan, no matter how it is implemented in the future, it can at least further promote Sino-British economic relations. In addition, Lord Rothermere, the giant of the British press, traveled to the Far East earlier this month and strongly advocated in telegrams back to Britain that Britain should rapidly increase assistance to Far Eastern trade and shipping. Judging from the attitude of the British government and public towards Far Eastern issues, we feel that Britain's current self-defense for its own interests indeed has a fairly consistent relationship of interests with our self-defense for national survival. The evolution of its Far East policy is something we cannot ignore.

Looking at the historical process, Britain once dominated the Chinese market. However, since the European War, it has suffered a series of severe blows. The termination of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance was clearly due to its own deep awareness that raising a tumor leaves trouble behind. Since the September 18th Incident, not only has its interests in China been shaken, but even the British territories in India, Australia, and the Nanyang region have become targets of the Far Eastern island nation. This seems to have been unexpected by the British. Britain today cannot be without the intention of mending the fold after losing the sheep.

Although Britain has long had the emblem of a nine-tailed fox on the world diplomatic stage, after Ross stumbled several times and was given the cold shoulder, it first signed a naval agreement with the Soviet Union, and then implemented currency cooperation with France and the United States. It is clearly seeking to defend and attack in the Far Eastern market. From Britain's standpoint, this "defense as offense" strategy is for temporary security. From Japan's point of view, it has become a major obstacle that it yearns to break through.

The position our country is currently in is crystal clear. We should recognize the keynote of British Far East policy and determine an appropriate diplomatic path. Only in this way can we prevent the disruption of peace in the Far East and save our national crisis.

Salvaging the World Situation: France and Russia Expand Their Air Forces; Russia Takes Japan and Germany as Standards; France Builds More Than 1,000 New-Type Aircraft; US Air Force Begins Pacific Maneuvers

(Paris) The cabinet held a cabinet meeting this morning and approved the air force replenishment plan proposed by Aviation Minister Cot, which requires an estimated expenditure of 5,000,000,000 francs. The content is divided into five items: (1) Accelerate the manufacture of aircraft, the number of which should be more than the original plan of 1,000 aircraft, and their power should be greater than the original plan; (2) Add aircraft fields and expand the existing aircraft fields; (3) Increase gasoline storage and improve the armament equipped for each aircraft; (4) Increase the number of air force personnel; (5) National aircraft manufacturing experimental sites should be concentrated near Chalon in the Provence region in the south. The cabinet then discussed the budget for 1937 and unanimously approved the report submitted by Finance Minister Auriol. According to the plan set by the Minister of Finance, the business tax rate should be reduced, and the tax rate should be increased for those with an annual income of more than 60,000 francs. The cabinet also decided to hold a state council meeting at 5 pm to discuss the diplomatic situation and determine the date for the resumption of Congress, which is expected to be November 3 or November 5. (Havas, 27th)

(London) It was learned here today that the Soviet Union is currently formulating an air force plan based on the standards of the two countries. Once this plan is completed, the Soviet air force will be sufficient to cope with Japan and Germany simultaneously. The Soviet Union's sudden expansion of its air force is due to Germany's emphasis on setting up defenses in the Rhineland, which hinders French troops from assisting Russia, thus weakening Russia's military position and promoting the fascist bloc in Europe. (National, 26th)

(London) Since Germany and Italy jointly established a common anti-communist front, expressing their intention to overthrow communism, the left-wing camp on the European continent will soon fall. It is reported that the Soviet government, from the perspective of salvaging the general situation, has established a two-country standard plan for the air force, and has decided to move towards the realization of the air force advantages of Germany and Japan. As for the Soviet government's attempt to implement the two-country standard plan, the following are listed:

(1) Since Germany decided to implement the re-equipment of the Rhineland, the Soviet government has difficulty expecting the assistance of the French National Army;

(1) Since the European dictatorship group has strengthened, the hostile forces against the Soviet Union have become more powerful;

(1) The British government seems to be attempting to get closer to the German government;

(1) Since the Belgian government declared neutrality, the position of the French army has been weakened. (Allied, 26th)

Honolulu Forty US Navy aircraft, led by Admiral King, flew from Pearl Harbor Naval Base into the central Pacific today in the rain to conduct unprecedented solo maneuvers. Admiral King kept the details of the exercise secret, only saying that the exercise site was a large triangle between Honolulu, Midway Island, and Palmyra Island. However, some people speculate that these aircraft may fly to Baker Island, Howland Island, and Jarvis Island. Commander Wedding and four staff officers departed on aircraft VP·4. Forty-one naval aviation base officers and 120 aviators took the remaining aircraft, and 800 soldiers were on board the aircraft carrier "Wright" (National, 26th)

Japan Operates Aviation in Mandated Islands; Submits Annual Report to League of Nations

(Geneva) Japan's annual report to the League of Nations Mandate Committee, disclosed today, stated that aviation routes have been opened between the islands of the South Pacific. The first line, connecting Palau Island and Saipan Island, was established in 1935, and other aviation routes are already being planned. (National, 26th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Commission on Mandates held its 30th session this morning, chaired by Belgian representative Orts. The discussions were on (1) the Japanese government's annual report on the Caroline, Marshall, and Mariana Islands under mandate; (2) the French government's report on the Togo mandate in Central Africa. (Havas, 27th)

Aviation Race Between Paris and Saigon; Two Aircraft Withdraw Mid-way; Only One Aircraft Remains En Route

(Paris) In the aviation race from Paris to Saigon, 14,000 miles, only one of the three participating aircraft, piloted by Charles and Biel, remains en route. The aircraft piloted by Arnoux and Yopi withdrew from the race yesterday when it landed in Karachi due to damage to the fuselage. The aircraft piloted by Testroja and Darman was forced to land in Kaurinz yesterday due to lack of fuel. After refueling, it continued to move forward. It arrived safely in Baghdad at 12:46 pm yesterday, and then departed again after forty minutes. After not hearing any news of the aircraft for 24 hours, Teste suddenly sent a telegram from Bushire saying that he and his companion had decided to abandon the race and are now returning home via Damascus. The reason for the abandonment was not stated. The aircraft piloted by Charles and Biel encountered danger in Lyon yesterday due to engine damage, but their ambition was not discouraged. This morning, they returned to the Le Bourget airfield. Because the radio operator was sick, they replaced him with another person and set off again at 10:31 am. Before leaving, they said that although they lost two days of time, they still hoped to break the record (Reuters, 27th)

Britain Increases Far East Air Force Strength; Five Airships Head to Singapore

Basra Five airships that took off from England on October 16 for Singapore departed from here today to continue their unfinished journey. According to reports, this airship team is led by Commander Dunn. The purpose of this flight to Singapore is to increase the strength of the Royal Air Force in the Far East. (Reuters, 26th)

US Army Purchases 100 Trainer Aircraft

(Washington) The Department of the Army announced today that the United States recently purchased 117 low-wing trainer aircraft with single engines and 400 horsepower from the North American Aviation Company in California for a total price of $1,432,600. US and Germany Launch Transatlantic Aviation

(Berlin) Gablenz, technical director of Lufthansa, announced today that a contract has been signed with Pan American Airways to launch a transatlantic air route. Two German aircraft have already flown across the Atlantic Ocean eight times, and the United States has approved ten more flights next year. British Imperial Airways has also approved German aircraft to pass through northern Ireland. (National, 26th)

(New York) Pan American Airways officials stated today that they have not heard of any contract being signed with Lufthansa. (National, 26th)

Anglo-Russian Naval Agreement; Britain Makes Concessions to Russia; Germany Expresses Dissatisfaction

(Paris) Regarding the naval agreement recently negotiated between the British government and the Soviet Union, it is rumored that Britain has made many concessions. Labrouye, the naval reporter for Le Petit Parisien, recently declared that Germany has notified Britain that the points that Britain intends to concede are said to conflict with the London Naval Treaty of the three countries of Britain, France, and the United States (signed in March 1936) and the Anglo-German Naval Agreement (signed in June 1935). If this is true, Germany will declare the Anglo-German Naval Agreement terminated. The reporter also said that the main clauses contained in the new London Naval Treaty of Britain, France, and the United States include two types. One is that the signatory countries should notify each other of the warship construction procedures. The second is that each item has quality restriction measures, but this clause cannot take effect unless all naval countries participate unanimously. After the establishment of the new naval treaty, the reason why Britain contacted Germany and the Soviet Union separately was because of this. Later, when Germany and Britain conducted negotiations, Germany agreed to accept this clause, but raised several reservations regarding the Soviet Navy, especially the Soviet Far East Fleet, believing that the armaments equipped by Soviet warships were newer than the most advanced warships in Western European countries and that it possessed the world's most powerful submarine fleet, with a total of 120 large submarines and 20 more under construction. In addition, the Soviet Union argued that it had the right to build seven Class A cruisers (10,000 tons displacement), all equipped with 180mm caliber guns (because Russian technicians are accustomed to working with this caliber). All of this is not allowed by the qualitative restriction measures of the new naval treaty (this measure prohibits the construction of cruisers over 8,000 tons and does not allow the equipment of guns with a caliber of more than 155mm). Germany has not approved it, and the Soviet Union is allowed to monopolize its advantages. In addition, the Soviet Union used Japan's failure to participate in the new naval treaty as an excuse to claim that it had the right to build warships freely in the Far East. In this way, it is not difficult for the country to expand its Far East fleet and transfer the newly built ships to the Baltic Sea, the Mediterranean Sea, and the Black Sea at any time. In Germany, according to the Anglo-German Naval Agreement, its total fleet tonnage should be limited to 35% of the total tonnage of the British Navy, which is naturally behind the Soviet fleet. Regarding the tonnage figures of the Soviet submarine fleet, the naval reporter for Le Petit Parisien believes that Germany is exaggerating. Although the three Soviet battleships have recently been renovated and equipped with new armaments, this is no different from what other countries have done to refit old battleships, and there is no need to pay special attention to it. (Havas, 27th)

A Page in the British King's Love History Over the Past Two Years; Daily Gifts of Fresh Flowers to His Girlfriend; Mrs. Simpson Granted Divorce from Her Husband

(London) It was learned here today that King Edward has been sending his girlfriend, Mrs. Simpson, roses worth £5 every day for the past two years. (National, 26th)

Ipswich The divorce case between Mrs. Simpson, a friend of King Edward, and her husband was heard in court here today and was granted a divorce in just ten minutes. According to the grounds for divorce filed by Mrs. Simpson, her husband was unfaithful, and two waiters testified as witnesses, but who her husband had an affair with was not disclosed. (National, 27th)

(London) It was learned here today that the Archbishop of Canterbury has decided to decline to preside over the King's coronation ceremony next year because the public may misunderstand that the bishop has ignored the relationship between King Edward and Mrs. Simpson. This decision is said to be of a "personal" nature, because the bishop is the religious advisor to Queen Mary and the leader of the Church of England, which is different from the position of the Archbishop of York. If the Archbishop of Canterbury insists on this, then Edward's coronation ceremony next year may be presided over by the Archbishop of York. However, if this happens, it will attract worldwide attention. (National, 26th)

A Team of British Sailors Insulted by Japanese Police in Taiwan; British Fleet Commander Postpones Trip to Japan

(London) It is learned that the commander-in-chief of the British fleet stationed in China, Vice Admiral Little, has postponed his trip to Japan. The reason is currently being investigated locally. The Admiralty heard news that an unfortunate incident between Britain and Japan had occurred again in Keelung, Taiwan, and telegraphed to inquire about the truth. The simple reply was that a small team of sailors from the British submarine supply ship Medway, 15,000 tons, had landed in Keelung to relax and were suspected by Japanese police of taking pictures of a fortified area. They were all taken to the police station for questioning. It is said that before being released, they were treated rudely. After the search, it was found that the suspicion was completely unfounded. However, the British authorities have not received a written explanation or apology from the Japanese side. This matter has been negotiated with the Japanese government through diplomatic channels. (Reuters, 27th)

(London) A well-informed source here recently declared that the British fleet in the Far East was originally scheduled to visit Japan this year, but Fleet Commander Little has postponed the date of the visit. The reason should be sought in this matter. Officials said that the British government had reason to lodge a formal protest. The postponement of the Far East fleet's visit to Japan shows the seriousness of the case. (Havas, 27th)

Belgian Party Strife; Socialist Party Demands the Suppression of Fascism

Brussels The Socialist Party Congress continued yesterday and passed a resolution stating that because domestic groups that endanger national security are supported by foreign countries, the party specifically requests the government to take strict measures immediately to stop them. The Socialist Party has always accused the fascist Rexist Party of accepting German money, but has not presented any evidence to substantiate its claim. The resolution passed this time seems to be aimed at the Rexist Party. (Havas, 27th)

Brussels During the demonstration held by the fascist Rexist Party the day before yesterday, leader Degrelle was arrested by the police and was not released until yesterday morning. Degrelle then gave a speech to 600 party members in the evening, saying, "The demonstration the day before yesterday was a great success. The outside world said that there were only 5,000 people participating, but there were actually 50,000. I will ask the government to allow the party to hold another rally. At that time, the number of participants can reach 400,000. From this, it will not be difficult to recruit the people of the whole country." He then reported on his arrest, saying that he had stayed in a house on Saint Gudule Square on Saturday and Sunday in order to avoid the eyes and ears of the government and did not go out, hoping to give a speech to the crowd the next day, but he was still arrested by the police. Degrelle now plans to go to various provinces to continue his propaganda movement, but the detailed plan has not been announced. (Havas, 27th)

Riots Erupt Again in Bombay

Bombay After three days of relative calm, disturbances occurred here today. It is reported that there were eight cases of assault, six of which occurred at night. Riots broke out here earlier due to conflicts between Hindus and Muslims, which lasted for a week and then subsided. A total of 61 people died, more than 500 were injured, and more than 1,300 were arrested by the police. During the riots, hundreds of shops were robbed, and the fire brigade was dispatched 71 times. (Reuters, 26th)

Philippine President's Visit to China Postponed

(Manila) President Quezon announced today that his visit to China has been postponed indefinitely due to busy political affairs. (National, 26th)

Failure of the Spanish Government Army's Final Counteroffensive; Rebels Were Once on the Verge of Collapse; Airstrikes Were Instrumental in Turning the Tide

Talavera: Government militias launched a fierce counteroffensive 18 miles southwest of Madrid against Navalcarnero. After a day of fierce fighting, the Nationalist forces repelled the militias. During the battle, for two hours, the defending forces seemed on the verge of collapse. The militias began their offensive at dawn with heavy artillery bombardment, one force advancing from the north and another from the south, attempting to encircle the town. Nationalist commander Colonel Asensio could only respond to the frontal assault with a few mortars and machine guns, unable to attend to the flanks. The situation was dire. Fortunately, the air force responded to the call and strafed the militias with bombs and machine-gun fire, averting disaster. Simultaneously, the government's encircling column was about to converge on the highway to Valmojado behind Navalcarnero. Then, a detachment of Moroccan and foreign legion troops arrived at the rear, and with the aid of aircraft, defeated the besieging militias. It is now believed that this was the government army's final counteroffensive. According to several military observers, the Madrid garrison is exhausted, and the city may fall within a week. (Reuters, 26th)

Madrid: A special dispatch from our correspondent reports that government forces launched an offensive against the Nationalist forces near the city of Navalagamella, southwest of the capital, yesterday and have achieved victory, advancing to within four kilometers of the city's outskirts. Their left flank, under the cover of light tanks and field guns, even advanced to within 200 meters of the city walls. Many of the shells hit their mark, setting many houses in the city on fire. The government army headquarters has now ordered a temporary halt to the advance to avoid being exploited by the Nationalist forces, resulting in the undoing of previous gains. (Havas, 27th)

Saint-Jean-de-Luz: Basque militias attacked Nationalist revolutionary army positions in Mañaria, 20 miles east of Bilbao, today, but were repulsed, suffering over 200 casualties. The Nationalist revolutionary army warships "España" and "Velasco" are reportedly patrolling the Bay of Biscay, severing maritime traffic between Bilbao and Le Havre. (Reuters, 26th)

Barcelona: Catalan forces have occupied the Púgdalba area, bringing the communication lines between Tárrega, Alcoberro, and Zaragoza under their control. Government forces claim that the Nationalist revolutionary army has been repulsed before Tárrega. (Reuters, 26th)

Talavera: According to a Nationalist forces press officer, the ring around Madrid is tightening. Nationalist forces have occupied Guadarrama, a town on the Madrid-Sigüenza highway, bringing the eastern Nationalist forces front to within 35 miles of the city. Nationalist aircraft bombed Madrid's barracks and railways again today, and destroyed the civilian airfield in Barajas. For the first time since the outbreak of the civil war, Madrid's shortwave radio station did not broadcast any news last night. (Reuters, 27th)

(Paris) According to the Morning Post's report from Hengtai, Soviet Ambassador to Spain, Rosenberg, reported to Moscow today that the Spanish government forces could not defend the capital, and their position was untenable. (National Telegram, 26th)

Madrid: Prime Minister Caballero, Foreign Minister Vayo, and Naval and Air Minister Prieto met today and decided to defend the capital outside the city. Cabinet members believe that the frontline defenses a few miles outside the capital should be manned by battle-hardened veterans, the second line of defense by the Guardia Civil, and the workers as reserves. The rebels have not advanced in recent days, so the cabinet hopes to build defensive fortifications outside the city. (National Telegram, 26th)

Russian and Italian Arms Supplies to Spain

(London) The Daily Express recently published a front-page headline with news from their correspondent in Istanbul, Turkey, stating that last week, 23 Soviet ships passed through the Dardanelles Strait, bound for the Mediterranean, 15 of which were carrying munitions openly to Spain. For example, the "Garl Libin" carried two aircraft and 500 tons of military equipment to Cartagena, Spain; the "Terens Balter" carried six aircraft, 70 trucks, 1,500 tons of ammunition, and 2,000 tons of food and medical supplies to Barcelona; and the "Shakto" carried a batch of military equipment to Alicante. (Havas, 27th)

(London) Rumors that the Soviet freighters "Volga," "Siberia," and "Leningrad" had transported munitions through the Dardanelles Strait to Barcelona, Spain, have been vehemently denied by the Soviet Embassy in the UK. It is claimed that the "Volga" is currently undergoing repairs in Dover, England; the "Siberia" departed London on the 17th of this month and has already arrived in Leningrad, loading cargo; and the "Leningrad" was built in 1889, is very old, and can only sail along the Black Sea coast, never having sailed outside the Black Sea. (Havas, 27th)

Istanbul, Turkey: Rumors that several Soviet warships had recently passed through the Bosporus and Dardanelles straits into the Mediterranean have been denied by Turkish officials. They stated that if Soviet warships were to enter the Mediterranean from the Black Sea, they would have to obtain permission from the Turkish government before passing through the straits, according to the new Straits Convention established at the Montreux Conference in July. However, the Soviet Union has not recently submitted such a request to Turkey, indicating that the claim of their warships passing through the straits is inaccurate. However, it is true that several Soviet freighters have passed through the straits into the Mediterranean. Some of their cargo was grain, and the contents of others are unknown. Furthermore, these freighters claimed to be sailing to Mexico, but after 12 to 15 days, they returned to the Black Sea, indicating that their voyage did not extend beyond the Mediterranean. (Havas, 27th)

(Paris) According to today's newspaper, eight Italian submarines, commanded by Italians but manned by Spanish sailors and flying the Spanish flag, are prepared to depart from northern Italy today to attack Catalonia. Fifteen German submarines reportedly passed through the Strait of Gibraltar on October 19th to assist Italy in blockading Catalonia. (National Telegram, 26th)

Six Governments Exist Within Spain; Portugal Recognizes Rebel Government

(London) There are now six governments in Spain. According to a Paris dispatch, the militias stationed in Bujaraloz, 37 miles southeast of Zaragoza, declared the autonomy of Aragon today and have established a provisional government. However, the old capital of the state, Zaragoza, remains in the hands of the Nationalist revolutionary army. There are also rumors that Cordoba, north of Seville, has declared independence, and that Basque nationalists have established a provisional government in Bilbao. Burgos, the headquarters of the Nationalist revolutionary army, and Madrid and Barcelona, which have had autonomous governments since the overthrow of the monarchy, each have independent governments. (Reuters, 27th)

(London) The Foreign Office announced today that Portugal has recognized the Spanish Nationalist forces government as the legitimate government. The Foreign Office has received notification of this. (National Telegram, 27th)

(London) Since severing diplomatic relations with the Madrid government of Spain, rumors have circulated that Portugal has recently recognized the Nationalist forces government in Burgos, Spain. Responsible officials here have neither confirmed nor denied this rumor. (Havas, 27th)

Lisbon: An official statement was issued here today, explaining the reasons for Portugal's severing of diplomatic relations with Spain, and publishing the full text of the note from the Portuguese government to the Spanish ambassador in Lisbon. The note is divided into six sections. The first section states that the Madrid government sent a note to Portugal on September 15th, accusing it of aiding the rebels, but without providing any supporting documentation. The Madrid side reported this matter to the Non-Intervention Adjustment Committee and the League of Nations without waiting for a response from the Portuguese government. The second section states that the Portuguese chargé d'affaires protested to the Spanish government, saying that it had privately inspected Portuguese diplomatic documents. However, according to the Spanish government's reply, future diplomatic correspondence would not be guaranteed. The third section criticizes Spain for searching Portuguese diplomatic pouches containing diplomatic documents. The fourth section mentions that authorities in Tarragona displayed hostility when Portuguese ships transported Spanish refugees back to their country. The fifth section states that the Spanish ambassador in Lisbon fabricated rumors that he had been isolated within the embassy, as if under house arrest. The main point of the sixth section is that, in view of the above facts, it is impossible for Portugal to maintain amicable relations with the Madrid government. The Portuguese chargé d'affaires in Spain has received instructions to leave Spanish territory immediately. (Reuters, 27th)

Joint Conference of International Labor Organizations Decides to Aid Spain and Prevent Supplies to the Rebels

(Paris) The International Federation of Trade Unions and the Labor International convened a joint conference here today and passed a resolution calling on the governments of Britain and France to take steps to restore freedom of trade with the Spanish government because the non-intervention agreement had failed. The conference also resolved to invite trade unions around the world to join together to prevent supplies to the Nationalist revolutionary army in Spain. (Reuters, 26th)

Romanian King Visits Czechoslovakia Accompanied by Crown Prince and Foreign Minister

Bucharest, Romania: King Carol II, accompanied by Crown Prince Michael and Foreign Minister Antonescu, departed for Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, yesterday to attend the country's National Day celebration. The local newspaper "River Te Weir Lur" recently published speeches by King Carol, former Foreign Minister Titulescu, Czech President Beneš, and Yugoslav Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Stojadinović, all emphasizing the vitality of the Little Entente. King Carol said, "The most pleasing thing about this trip is the clear demonstration of the unity and indivisibility of the Little Entente countries." Czech President Beneš said, "The political organization established by the Little Entente countries originates from an idea: that we can work and help each other with confidence and possess great power, willing to participate in European politics with full rights." Yugoslav Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Stojadinović declared, "The basic principles of the South's foreign policy remain two: maintaining the most friendly relations with allied countries, and maintaining normal relations with neighboring countries." Former Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu said that the achievements of the Little Entente demonstrated the great effectiveness of establishing regional self-defense based on the principle of mutual assistance and within the framework of the League of Nations. (Havas, 27th)

Italy and Germany Decide to Maintain the Status Quo in the Western Mediterranean; Spain Will Not Cede Islands

(London) According to the communiqué issued by Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano in Schongau, Germany, yesterday, Italy and Germany have agreed to maintain the original sovereignty over the Spanish Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean. Political circles here are very pleased with this news and believe that the guarantee previously made by the Spanish Nationalist forces government that it would not cede the Balearic Islands to Italy or the Canary Islands to Germany is now credible after the publication of the Schongau communiqué. Political circles also stated that Italy and Germany have not reached a consensus on how to respond to the Soviet Union's stance on the issue of non-intervention in the Spanish civil war. Germany advocates adopting a peaceful approach to maintain the existence of the Non-Intervention Adjustment Committee. (Havas, 26th)

German Ambassador to the UK Begins His Term by Focusing on Anti-Communism; Advocates Cooperation Between the Two Countries

(London) The new German Ambassador to the UK, Ribbentrop, arrived in London today. Reportedly, the German leader Hitler believes that the continued spread of communism is the only real danger to Europe and the British Empire. For the sake of jointly striving to maintain German and British culture, the two countries should cooperate closely. When Ribbentrop alighted at Victoria Station, leaders of the German community in London, wearing formal attire and tall hats, waved to Ribbentrop and gave the Nazi salute. (Reuters, 26th)

(London) After the arrival of the new German Ambassador Ribbentrop, many newspapers extended a welcome, saying that there was hope for an improvement in relations between Britain and Germany. However, the Daily Telegraph, a Conservative newspaper, and the News Chronicle, a Liberal newspaper, both expressed surprise at Ribbentrop's statement to the press yesterday that communism was a real threat to peace in Europe. The Daily Telegraph wrote, "It is regrettable that Ambassador Ribbentrop, at the beginning of his term, spoke of the dangers of communism and called for close cooperation between Britain and Germany, because there are even more compelling reasons why Britain and Germany should reach an understanding." The News Chronicle wrote, "If Ambassador Ribbentrop wants to promote a good understanding between Britain and Germany, he needs to find another way, and not rashly embark on a crusade against Russia." US Election Campaign Intensifies; Landon Spares No Effort in Attacking Roosevelt; Accuses Him of Abusing Public Funds and Destroying People's Freedom

(New York) The current election campaign between President Roosevelt and Landon has reached its crucial stage. Roosevelt is currently in his White House office, busy drafting his final speeches, preparing to deliver them in Pennsylvania, New York, and neighboring states. Landon, meanwhile, is engaged in a speaking tour from the West Coast to the East Coast, having passed through Washington on his way to New York. He will make brief stops in various important cities along the way. President Roosevelt will depart from Washington tomorrow evening on his special train, intending to deliver speeches in New York, New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and Delaware. Roosevelt will begin his final campaign speeches at the 50th anniversary celebration of the Statue of Liberty in New York Harbor. A grand occasion is planned for October 31st at Madison Square Garden in New York. On the eve of the election, Roosevelt is expected to use radio broadcasts to make a final appeal for votes to the national public. At the same time, Landon, after a brief rest in California, will continue his eastward journey by train, making travel speeches. However, because his throat ailment has not fully recovered, a doctor is constantly attending him. Landon is scheduled to give an important speech in Philadelphia tonight and plans to deliver his final political views to the citizens of New York at Madison Square Garden on October 28th. Landon also intends to broadcast his speech on the radio on the eve of the election. (Reuters, 26th)

Philadelphia, USA: Republican presidential candidate Landon said in a speech here today that President Roosevelt was openly wasting the people's money, violating the Constitution to oppress voters, and infringing on the privileges of the states, destroying individual freedom, and making the country a dictatorship with power concentrated in the President alone. The purpose of the Republican platform is to protect the Constitution and the lives of the American people, in order to prevent the New Deal from building an autocratic centralized government system. Landon also promised that if he were to take office, he would stop using the people's money for political activities and restore the position of the Budget Bureau, making it free from White House control, because the government should know that even a country as wealthy as the United States can be impoverished. Landon also said that people in Pennsylvania receiving government relief had received warnings that they would lose their relief funds if they did not re-elect President Roosevelt. Therefore, the weapons used by the current government are no different from the dictatorial governments in European countries that destroy people's freedom. The current government has seized the privilege of the House of Representatives to propose tax bills and the control of Congress over expenditures. People should know that the waste of the New Deal will ultimately be borne by the people. (National News Agency, 26th)

The market prices of securities are listed below.

Chicago Wheat: The opening price fell today. The unsettled European situation and the reduction in export demand were the reasons for limiting the development of market prices. Japanese Troops Stationed in North China Conduct Exercises: Sounds of Gunfire Heard Within Beijing on the 26th, Tensions Rise in Fengtai and Lugouqiao in the Western Suburbs

Beijing Dispatch: Following the increase of Japanese troops stationed in North China, their first major exercise commenced on the 26th. This day involved separate exercises by each regiment. The Tianjin contingent exercised in the vicinity of Tianjin, while the Beijing contingent exercised near Beijing. The Hebei-Chahar Pacification Commissioner's Office, the Foreign Affairs Committee, and the 29th Army Military Department all dispatched liaison officers to collaborate with the local police stations in the exercise areas, responsible for providing assistance. Matters such as the Japanese troops' encampment locations and the procurement of fodder, food, and other supplies were all handled by the liaison officers. The Japanese troops participating in the exercise began moving and concentrating separately from the 25th, using special trains provided by the Beijing-Shanhaiguan Railway for transportation. It is reported that one train of soldiers arrived in Tianjin from Shanhaiguan that day, and two trains arrived in Fengtai from Tianjin on the morning of the 26th. At 3:00 PM, one train departed from Fengtai for Tongzhou. It is scheduled that two trains will depart from Beijing via Dongbianmen on the 27th, and one train will arrive in Beijing from Tianjin. On the 28th, it is scheduled that two trains will depart from Tongzhou for Fengtai. In the Beijing area, the locations traversed by the Japanese troops' exercise were the eastern, southern, and western suburbs, as well as Lugouqiao, which belongs to Wanping, and Dahongmen, which belongs to Daxing. The situation on the 26th is recorded as follows:

According to the exercise schedule, a regimental exercise will be held in Shubao (20 li from Shuzhimen) in the eastern suburbs on the 27th. Our side has already selected encampment locations in advance at locations such as Princess Tomb, Yongjia Tomb, South Shijia Tomb, Songjia Tomb, and the Three Saints Temple. The Japanese troops will set up tents and not borrow civilian housing. On the morning of the 26th, more than 50 Japanese troops stationed in Beijing had already gone to these locations to prepare everything and camped there that night. The Japanese troops who arrived in Fengtai on the morning of the 26th and a portion of the Japanese troops in Tongzhou, totaling about 2,300 people, also transferred to Dongba. A small-scale regimental exercise was conducted that day, and sounds of gunfire could be faintly heard within the city. The southern suburbs were unaffected because Fengtai was the boundary of the Japanese troops' exercise area. Twenty Japanese troops stationed in Beijing took two heavy trucks at 9:00 AM on the 26th to transport military supplies. They planned to go to Fengtai via You'anmen, but because the road was difficult, they turned back to Yongdingmen and exited the city southward. At about 4:00 PM, the same trucks returned to the city.

In the western suburbs, the Japanese troops are scheduled to concentrate and camp on the 3rd of next month, and exercise and review troops at Babaoshan, 20 li west of Fuchengmen, on the 4th. The encampment locations prepared by our side in the western suburbs are major temples such as Baiyun Temple, Wanshou Temple, Tianning Temple, and Yuanguang Temple, without renting civilian houses. The Western Suburbs District also notified residents not to be alarmed at that time and not to go out to watch without reason. At 7:00 AM on the 26th, more than 400 Japanese troops stationed in Beijing, led by Kawamura, formed a team and exited Xibianmen, passing through the Shifangyuan area of the western suburbs and crossing the Pinghan Railway to exercise west of Lugouqiao in Wanping, launching an offensive towards Lugouqiao. After completing the exercise, they went to Kantan, west of Juetai, to rest and camped in Fengtai that night. On the morning of the 27th, they set off for Dongba. Another group of 460 Japanese troops stationed in Beijing, carrying two large cannons, one heavy cannon, and twenty-one machine guns, exited Guang'anmen at about 11:00 AM on the 26th and went to Lugouqiao via Xiaolin Village in the western suburbs to exercise. At about 4:00 PM, they all returned to Beijing. Along the way, they showed off their military strength, and many people watched. More than 20 Japanese soldiers went to Tiancun. The western suburbs were full of Japanese troops all day on the 26th. In Fengtai, more than 1,000 Japanese soldiers gathered on the drill ground outside the camp on the morning of the 26th and then set off for Lugouqiao to exercise. At about 3:00 PM, 520 Japanese troops remaining in Fengtai went to Tongzhou to exercise. At 5:00 PM, the Japanese troops who had gone to Lugouqiao returned to Jue. Another infantry force of 600 people then marched to Beijing. In Fengtai, in addition to those stationed in the barracks, a total of 290 people lived in inns and lecture halls such as Renhe, Yuelai, Jinfeng, and Heshun. The office was located in the Fengtai Chamber of Commerce. Most of the local residents kept their doors closed and did not go out. Red paper strips were pasted on civilian houses and shops, with the words "Do Not Enter" written on them.

At Lugouqiao, from 4:00 AM to 6:00 AM on the morning of the 26th, 430 infantrymen from the 3rd Battalion of the 1st Column of Japanese troops stationed in Fengtai, led by Battalion Commander Kiyoshi Ichiki, arrived and exercised in the area west of the Daishi Bridge. At 8:30 AM, another 460 people arrived from Beijing, carrying machine guns and steel cannons. They crossed the Lugouqiao in two batches and gathered at the Daishi Bridge, then divided into two groups to conduct confrontational exercises. One group of 200 people was in the southeast, and one group of 400 people was in the southwest. The two sides conducted offensive and defensive battles. At 9:40 AM, 40 artillerymen and 40 cavalrymen continued to arrive from Fengtai, carrying four steel cannons, and joined the exercise. At about 10:00 AM, another 200 infantrymen arrived and also joined the exercise. This exercise was a confrontation between the 10th Battalion and the 3rd Battalion of the 1st Regiment. The sound of gunfire could be heard within 20 li for a time. At noon, they picnicked in various locations. In the afternoon, they continued the exercise until about 2:00 PM, when they completed it and returned to Fengtai separately. One group of 600 people returned to Beijing and still lived in the Japanese barracks. The Political Council, the Pacification Office, and the 29th Army Observation Group, Zhou Yongye and others, followed them to observe. In the afternoon, after the Japanese troops returned to Beijing and Fengtai, they returned to Beijing (26th).

Suspicion Among a Certain Party: Status of Bandit and Puppet Troops in Northern Chahar

Wang's Bandit Troops' Brigade Commander Zhang Detained Suddenly; Bao, Zhuo, Zhang, and Li Consult in Zhangbei; A Certain Party Strictly Checks Travelers and Prohibits Reading Newspapers

Zhangbei Dispatch: Since the Jiabusi Conference, the bandit and puppet armies in northern Chahar have been clamoring to unite and advance westward, attempting to invade eastern Suiyuan. However, ten days have passed, and apart from occasional minor skirmishes along the Chahar-Suiyuan border, no major uprisings have been seen. The reason for this is that the puppet bandit troops feel insecure due to the whims of the figures behind the scenes; happiness brings unexpected rewards, but anger could mean loss of position and wealth. Therefore, their own organizations are not very sound, and their troop numbers and military strength are still being expanded, so they have been slow to act.

Bandit and Puppet Leaders Gather in Zhangbei

According to those familiar with the situation in northern Chahar, after Wang Ying was suspected by a certain party, there will be a major reshuffle soon. The title of Commander of the Puppet Anti-Communist Autonomous Army will also be abolished along with Wang Ying. His former puppet deputy commander, Zhang Wanqing, formerly Wang Ying's infantry brigade commander, whose troops numbered about two brigades, has been dismissed. In addition, Zhang, a brigade commander under Wang, came to Zhangbei from Shangdu a few days ago to arrange for the receipt of military supplies and provisions. For some reason, he was suddenly detained by a certain party. Li Shouxin's troops have moved in large numbers from Zhangbei to the northwest in recent days and are currently stalled in the Daqinggou area. Li himself is still in Zhangbei, meeting with Niu Yangqun Banner King Zhuo Shihai, Right Wing Pastoral Group General Manager Selengnabenjile (named Yongcheng), and Zhang HaiPeng, a rebel, for several days to discuss certain matters. It is also said that the former Bordered Yellow Banner General Manager Mukdengbao (i.e., Mu Guihua) will take over as commander of the 7th Division of the puppet Mongolian army. His troops stationed in Kangbao, numbering about several hundred, will soon be stationed in Jiabusi. The Kangbao area they leave behind will be taken over by Bao Yueqing's troops. The Mongolian puppet armies have been changing frequently recently. Since Wang Ying's title of Commander of the Puppet Anti-Communist Autonomous Army has been abolished, a certain party has now approved the reorganization of his troops into a cavalry division, with Wang Ying still serving as commander. Liu Zhiqian and Jin Niansan will serve as brigade commanders. The division will be composed of approximately two brigades, or possibly three.

Replenishing Military Supplies, Purchasing Coal Bricks

Li Shouxin's troops have been actively replenishing military supplies recently. Large quantities of military supplies, such as artillery shells, aircraft engines, and spare parts for vehicles, have been transported from a certain location to Zhangbei by heavy trucks in recent days, with ammunition and rifles being the most numerous. In addition, leather uniforms, gasoline, kerosene, wooden poles for supporting camps, and coal bricks are also numerous. Li is purchasing from Shanxi and a certain location within the Pass, but because the quantity he needs is too large, it is difficult to purchase all at once. On the 24th, more than 1,000 sets of saddles and more than 3,000 sets of military uniforms (both leather and cotton) purchased by Wang Ying's troops were loaded onto five heavy trucks and transported from a certain location through Zhangbei to Shangdu for the soldiers of Wang Ying's bandit troops to wear.

Checking Travelers, Restricting Miscellaneous Grains

The people of northern Chahar live a precarious existence under the iron heel of the puppet bandits, their difficulties reaching the extreme. Not only is their life unsustainable, but their freedom is also deprived. Even the right to read newspapers is not allowed; they are only allowed to read the Shengjing Times published within a certain party's camp. Apart from this, all newspapers from the interior are forbidden, and severe punishments are given if they are found. Therefore, the people are very isolated from national affairs. Currently, Zhangbei is strictly checking travelers; anyone who is slightly suspicious is either detained or expelled. Locals who want to leave the area must find a reliable shop as a guarantor, stating the time limit for their return, and are only allowed to travel after a certain party has issued a permit. This is particularly disadvantageous to the local people. The price of food in various places in northern Chahar has been soaring recently due to restrictions on grain purchases, especially in Kangbao and Baochang. Wheat has risen to 1.40 yuan per dou, and buckwheat is around 1.05 yuan per dou. In the past, one yuan could buy 30 to 40 jin of wheat flour, but the difference in value is more than tenfold. Cattle, sheep, and horses, which are major exports and resources for the people outside the Pass, are also under control. The export of horses is strictly prohibited, and merchants who come from afar within the Pass to purchase horses are suffering greatly. Currently, the price of cattle is around 40 yuan per head, and sheep are 3-4 yuan each. Many are imported every day (24th).

Jiangsu Province Celebrates Chairman Chiang's Birthday by Presenting Nine Aircraft: Naming Ceremony to be Held Tomorrow at Jurong Airport, Wang Boling Appointed as Chief Representative for Aircraft Presentation

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Branch of the Chinese Aviation Association has been actively preparing to raise funds from all sectors of Jiangsu Province to purchase aircraft to present to the government as a celebration of Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. It has now been decided that the naming ceremony will be held tomorrow (29th) at Jurong Airport. After the naming ceremony, the aircraft will fly directly to Nanjing for presentation. The details are as follows:

Preparation Process

The Jiangsu Aviation Association decided to raise funds from all sectors of Jiangsu Province to purchase aircraft to celebrate the birthday of Chairman Chiang, and proceeded separately through groups such as the Party, government, military, education, and business. The Party Department was responsible for urging contributions, the military, government, police, and judicial departments were responsible for urging contributions through the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the education sector was responsible for urging contributions through the Education Department, and the business sector was responsible for urging contributions through local chambers of commerce and the Provincial Federation of Commerce. The stipulated amount was 720,000 yuan, to purchase a squadron of aircraft (nine planes). The aircraft were purchased by the Central Government, and the funds were gradually remitted to the Central Government. More than 500,000 yuan has already been paid.

Enthusiastic Participation

Jiangsu Province will present nine aircraft, but the estimated fundraising results are only expected to yield more than 700,000 yuan, while each aircraft is valued at 100,000 yuan. This amount is only sufficient to purchase seven aircraft, and it seems somewhat lacking to not complete a squadron. The farmers, workers, boy scouts, and various freelance professions in the province have voluntarily and enthusiastically contributed to make up the shortfall, in order to fulfill the people's respect for the leader. There have also been quite a few individuals who have voluntarily donated.

Naming Ceremony

The aircraft presented by Jiangsu Province are scheduled to have their naming ceremony at 2:00 PM on the 29th of this month at the Jurong Airport, and the Jiangsu Provincial Aircraft Presentation and Birthday Celebration Naming Ceremony Preparatory Committee has been established. The committee has been working very hard in recent days. Yu Zhaoqi, a member of the preparation committee, went to Jurong yesterday to arrange everything. The naming of the nine aircraft has been determined to be (1) Jiangsu Merchant One, (2) Jiangsu Merchant Two, (3) Jiangsu Merchant Three, (4) Jiangsu Elementary School Student, (5) Jiangsu Faculty and Student, (6) Jiangsu Party and Government, (7) Jiangsu Political, Legal, Military, and Police, (8) Jiangsu Farmer and Worker, and (9) Jiangsu Boy Scout and Freelance Profession.

Invitation to Participate

The Preparatory Committee, in anticipation of this grand event, has previously sent letters to the governments, agencies, and groups in various counties, inviting them to send representatives to Jurong to participate. It also issued a public notice. Representatives from various counties participating in the aircraft presentation naming ceremony are to report to the temporary office of the committee in the Jurong County Government on the morning of the 29th. Those passing through Zhenjiang can report to the Security Office on the 28th. On the morning of the 29th, the committee will provide transportation to Jurong and has arranged with the Jiangsu-Jurong Railway to open a special train on that day to facilitate those attending.

Aircraft Presentation Representative

Jiangsu Province has appointed Committee Member Wang Boling as the plenipotentiary chief representative for the naming and presentation of the aircraft. After the naming ceremony in Jurong, he will fly to Nanjing for the presentation. Representatives from other provincial party and government agencies and agricultural, commercial, educational, military, police, and other groups will also be appointed to participate in the ceremony. Currently, those who have been appointed include Qiu Heqing, Secretary of the Civil Affairs Department, Yao Dechen, Secretary of the Finance Department, Xu Tigang, Secretary of the Construction Department, and Huang Shaohong, Secretary of the Education Department. Representatives from other agricultural, commercial, educational, and other groups will also be appointed.

Urging Contributions

The funds for the nine aircraft presented by Jiangsu Province were collected from various sources, so the contribution process is difficult to unify. The business community alone donated funds for three aircraft, which is sufficient to demonstrate the businessmen's enthusiastic support for the leader. However, because of the large number of donations, it is not easy to collect them all at once. It is reported that the Jiangsu Aviation Association, in addition to discussing with the responsible agencies to send personnel to urge the remittance of the more than 500,000 yuan that has already been remitted to the Central Government, hopes that the remaining amount can be collected and sent to the association in the near future so that it can be remitted to the Central Government.

Songjiang: Opening of First Aid Training

The Songjiang Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society is running a first aid training class with a quota of sixty students. Prepared by Director Zhou Xuewen, the opening ceremony is scheduled to be held at 2:00 PM on November 1st, at Chaoguo Temple outside the West Gate. Leaders from all sectors have been invited to visit at that time.

Agreed on Grain Collection Quality

This year's autumn harvest is bountiful, and the new grain is gradually appearing on the market. The quality of grain collected for rent is usually discussed and agreed upon at a meeting convened by the county government, attended by representatives from wealthy families and relevant agencies. This year's meeting was held at the county government on the afternoon of the 26th. The result was a decision to collect 7.7 dou of rent rice per stone of the standard rent. The authorities will issue a notice to the public within a few days.

Four Robberies in One Night Outside the North Gate

Li Wentian, a resident of the 7th household of the 27th Jia of the 1st Bao of Tongbo Township in Shishitu outside the North Gate, and two farmers from the same Bao, Li Wentian and Li Guanshou, were robbed by more than 20 bandits who broke into their homes at midnight on the 25th. The bandits all spoke in strong Hakka accent, wearing blue clothes and white short shirts and pants, with large hats and carrying rapid-fire guns and pistols. They first tied up Li Wentian and his wife, Gu, and beat them to force them to reveal their valuables, causing injuries. After stealing the valuables, they went to rob the homes of Li Jisheng and Zhang Honggen, two households of the 2nd household of the 5th Jia and the 3rd household of the 9th Jia of the same Bao. Before leaving, they injured Honggen and his wife, Shen, with wooden sticks and took the stolen goods, heading east along the Songsi Road. Afterwards, Li Wentian's family found that they had been robbed of 55 yuan in paper money, more than 20 bolts of native cloth, and two pieces of clothing. Li Guanshou's family was robbed of more than 10 bolts of native cloth, seven silver hairpins, two silver garlic sprout bracelets for children, 5 yuan in paper money, and 500 copper coins. Li Jisheng's family was robbed of a silver hairpin and dozens of pieces of clothing. Zhang Honggen's family was robbed of a gold bracelet, a gold ring, five bolts of native cloth, more than ten pieces of clothing, and three cotton quilts. The victims have filed a report with the Public Security First Sub-bureau, requesting an investigation.

Suzhou: Traitor Escorted to the Garrison Headquarters

The Public Security Bureau has recently arrested several suspected traitors who looked like beggars and are currently interrogating them. Yesterday, a man named Pu Yun was arrested on Banmenwai Avenue. Suspicious cards and bamboo chips were found on his person. The police station directly escorted him to the Public Security Bureau. After interrogation by the Third Section, he confessed that he was being used to come to Suzhou to gather certain information. Director Zhang, considering the matter to be related to treason, immediately escorted him to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.

Wuxi: Unresolved Warehouse Dispute

Xinshen No. 3 Factory has built a new Renhe warehouse on the open space west of the local railway station for loading and unloading goods. The contract was awarded to contractor Ding Ruixi. However, the workers of the railway warehouse believed that their business was being taken away and rose up in opposition, resulting in a dispute. The day before yesterday, a conflict almost broke out over the loading and unloading of jute bags. Section Chief Chen of the Xihu Police First Section intervened and dispatched police to suppress the situation, preventing a disaster. In order to resolve the matter properly, Section Chief Chen specially invited Station Master Yu Shucheng, Manager Tang Xiongyuan of the Xinren Warehouse, and Accountant Zhang Renshan to discuss solutions. Tang proposed that loading and unloading from the railway station to the warehouse would be handled by railway workers, and loading and unloading from the riverside pier to the warehouse would be handled by the warehouse's workers. Station Master Yu and others largely agreed. However, Ding Ruixi, the warehouse's contractor, stated that the railway workers could only go from the train to the warehouse entrance and not enter the warehouse, resulting in no resolution. Yesterday, the warehouse temporarily suspended the loading and unloading of goods for fear of another conflict, awaiting mediation.

Appealing Not to Increase Business Tax

The local Gold and Silver Industry Guild stated that the Jiangsu Finance Department's revised business tax regulations would increase the tax rate for jewelry stores from 10 per mille to 15 per mille. The jewelry store business relies on women's ornaments for sales. Since the popularity of women's haircuts in 1928, ornaments have been hit hard. Business has plummeted. After the January 28th Incident, the economy declined, rural areas went bankrupt, and the market became even more depressed. Paying taxes at the original rate is already an unbearable burden. If the tax rate is increased again, it would increase the burden on merchants and put the jewelry store industry in a dire situation. Therefore, they specially sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting them to forward it to the Finance Department, requesting that it withdraw its order and continue to levy taxes at the original rate of 10 per mille in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties.

Water and Land Public Security Conference

Zang Qifang, the Second District Administrative Inspector and Commissioner, believes that it is time for winter defense. The counties under his jurisdiction are located at the intersection of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, bordering both rivers and lakes, making them extremely important. All local security should be closely linked. Therefore, he convened a water and land public security conference this morning (28th). All district chiefs of the Provincial Water Public Security Corps Second District and the captains of the First, Second, Third, Fourth, and Fifth River Teams, the captains of the Jingping, Anjing, Peirong, and Jinghu warships stationed in Kunshan, Wuxian, Wuxi, and Wujiang counties, and the directors of the public security bureaus of Wuxi, Wujin, Wuxian, Wujiang, Changshu, Jiangyin, Kunshan, and Taicang counties all attended and participated in the discussion.

Changshu: Foreign Soldiers Land in Baimao

According to a phone call from Hupu, a shallow-water warship of a certain country arrived outside Hupu Port the day before yesterday afternoon to measure the water level and left in the evening. On the afternoon of the 26th, a warship of a certain country also arrived outside Baimao Port to conduct measurements and used a small boat to carry five or six soldiers ashore to drink tea in a teahouse. However, it was only for a short time, and they immediately boarded the boat and returned to the warship, sailing downstream. The local Public Security Bureau, seeing this situation, specially contacted the District Office and telegraphed the county government for instructions. Subsequently, the county government also discussed solutions and reported to the province for instructions.

Red Cross Trains First Aid Team

Yu Jiusi, Director of the local Red Cross Branch, believes that rescue workers are urgently needed in the YiLai (area). In order to cope with future events, thirty members have been selected for first aid training. The curriculum includes basic first aid knowledge, initial treatment, poison prevention, stretcher techniques, and artificial respiration. The opening ceremony was held this morning (27th) in the county government auditorium, and classes will begin in the afternoon. The duration is two months, and Shimei Elementary School has been designated as the lecture hall and the sports field as the training ground. Many members have requested training, and a second class will be held soon.

Jiangyin: Strange Guests Suddenly Arrive at Duanshan Port

Duanshan Port in the Third District Shazhou is a major Yangtze River port. A few days ago, five or six foreigners suddenly landed from a small boat, carrying a camera. They gave the brought biscuits to local cattle herding children, signaling them to eat. The children refused. They took pictures everywhere. The tax police stationed there, seeing their suspicious behavior but not understanding their language, could not stop them. They lingered for several hours and took the original boat to the east. The local Zhuangding (militia) team has reported this matter to higher-level agencies for investigation.

Nantong: Two Murderers Sentenced to Death

Cao Jintao, a farmer from Qinnian Township in Tongyi (Nantong), had an affair with Ji Caoshi, a young woman next door. Her husband, Ji Xiaobin, suddenly returned home from Shanghai. Cao Jintao and Ji Caoshi jointly strangled Ji Xiaobin, buried the body in the field, and eliminated the traces. The district office discovered the case and reported it. The two criminals were brought to court, and both confessed without hesitation. On the 26th, the criminal court concluded the trial. Ji Caoshi and Cao Jintao were each sentenced to death.

Reorganization of Private Intelligence Agency

The Ministry of Finance's pilot project for the Tongruhaichongqi District reconnaissance smuggling intelligence agency has received a telegram ordering reorganization. Director Gan Zhaoting has gone to Shanghai for instructions.

Gaoyou: Wheat Seedlings Damaged by Locusts

There has been no rain in the county for the past two months, and the drought is about to cause a disaster. Farmers in various townships are unable to sow seeds. Most are using manual labor or pumping water into the fields to facilitate the cultivation of winter wheat. They are hoping for rain day and night. Even the vegetable gardens in the city are difficult to grow due to the drought, causing prices to skyrocket. The low-lying fields in the eastern townships have already planted wheat seeds, but unexpectedly, locusts are rampant, and all the wheat seedlings have been eaten. Farmers are crying out in pain and must resow the seeds. In addition, the price of wheat is extremely high. No. 1 wheat in the county has reached 10.05 yuan, and secondary wheat has reached 10.03 yuan. In addition, the sauce gardens in the county traditionally pickle radish in the fall. Due to the drought, production has been greatly reduced, and prices have also risen, reaching more than one yuan per stone. All the stores are going to Huai'an and Baoying to purchase.

Removing Obstacles Along the Canal

The Yangqing Highway follows the canal bank. There are many obstacles along the canal, which pose a great danger to traffic. The highway administration has ordered the county to remove them, but it has not been done. The county government has appointed Jia Chengchun, the third section chief, and Yu Yunhu, the director of the first public security sub-bureau, to lead a team of police to the Cheqian area south of the county to persuade the removal of houses and other objects that obstruct traffic. Otherwise, they will be forcibly removed to facilitate traffic and ensure safety.

Cixi: Fundraising for Hongguan Road

The Cixi County Government believes that the funds for Cixi-Yang Road are insufficient, the project has been suspended, and efforts should be made to continue it. In order to facilitate transportation in the northern mountains, the planned construction of Hongguan Road should also be implemented. After the county magistrate convened a meeting of local gentry, it was decided that the construction of Hongguan Road would be funded by levying 0.35 yuan per mu of farmland in the northern mountains (totaling 17,000 mu), with the landowner bearing 0.25 yuan and the tenant bearing 0.1 yuan. The estimated construction cost is tentatively set at 60,000 yuan.

Hangzhou: Fresh Cocoons of Late Autumn Silkworms

The Zhejiang Cocoon and Silk Control Association has purchased more than 90,000 sheets of late autumn silkworm eggs this year and distributed them to various counties in western Zhejiang, including Haining, Haiyan, Chongde, Tongxiang, Wuxing, and Deqing, for rearing. They have now successively spun cocoons. However, due to the drought and dry mulberry leaves, the harvest of late autumn cocoons is only about 60%. The silk factories, due to the lack of raw materials, are enthusiastically requesting approval to register to purchase cocoons. The association has reviewed and approved the requests. The price of fresh cocoons is based on reeling yield, ranging from 30 to 33.8 yuan, and has been submitted to the provincial government for record. Recently, some early batches of fresh cocoons have appeared.

The Severity of Drought in Various Counties

Since the beginning of autumn in Zhejiang Province, there has been no rain for two months, resulting in an extreme drought. In the western counties of Zhejiang, due to the flat terrain and numerous rivers, the irrigation of late rice has not been significantly affected and harvesting is expected to begin early next month. While the harvest may not be abundant, the eastern counties of Zhejiang, with their more mountainous terrain and limited water sources, are experiencing severe water shortages. Rivers in the counties under Shaoxing Prefecture are gradually drying up, hindering navigation. Paddy fields are cracking due to the lack of water, causing significant damage to the late rice crop and preventing the planting of wheat. The drought is severely impacting agriculture. Furthermore, there is a shortage of drinking water in various counties, and the water is often unclean and turbid, leading to the rampant spread of epidemics.

Chinese Institute of Engineers Memorial Award Essay Contest

Annual Award Amount: 100 Yuan

Given to the Best Engineering Researcher: Zhu Qiqing, a member of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, has donated 1,000 yuan to the institute as a memorial award fund in memory of his late mother, Madam Gu. The "Zhu Mother Memorial Scholarship" will award 100 yuan annually to a Chinese scholar who has made outstanding achievements in engineering research and has written a paper on the subject. The essay contest has now begun, with a deadline of February 11th next year. The contest rules are as follows: (1) Eligibility: Any Chinese national, male or female, young or old, whether currently enrolled in school or engaged in self-study, who has a special interest in engineering research and wishes to participate, may apply. (2) Scope: Research in any field of engineering, regardless of the scope of the topic, is eligible. The format and style of the report are not restricted. (3) Award Amount and Number: The award is 100 yuan in cash, awarded annually to one winner. (4) Application Procedure: Applicants must first obtain an application form from the institute, complete it, and submit it to the institute for review. The application form and attachments should be sent by registered mail to the "Zhu Mother Memorial Scholarship Committee," Chinese Institute of Engineers, 5th Floor, Continental Emporium, Nanjing Road, Shanghai. (5) Judging: The Board of Directors of the Institute will appoint five judges to form a judging committee to oversee the judging process. (6) Deadline: The deadline for submissions is February 11th each year. The winner will be announced in the institute's Engineering Weekly. (7) Award Date: The scholarship will be awarded at the institute's annual meeting each year.

Zhejiang Education Department Orders Exhibition of History and Geography Achievements

The Zhejiang Education Department believes that history and geography education in primary and secondary schools is the most effective training for cultivating national culture, enriching international knowledge, understanding the current environment, and inspiring patriotism in young people. Therefore, when drafting the provincial education implementation plan for the 25th year of the Republic, it was included as a task to urge all secondary and normal schools to hold regional exhibitions of student achievements in history and geography, with the aim that both public and private secondary and normal schools will hold exhibitions of student achievements in history and geography within the year, so as to learn from each other and promote the subject. As the school year has already begun for almost two months, the above plan must be implemented. Inspectors have been instructed to discuss the implementation methods of the exhibition with the school authorities and history and geography teachers during their inspections. If regional exhibitions are difficult to organize immediately, each school can hold its own exhibition separately. After most schools have completed their exhibitions, the best exhibits can be selected by the schools to determine the location for a regional exhibition and prepare for it at a later date. This step-by-step approach is more economical in terms of manpower and resources, and the exhibition effect will be more comprehensive and lasting than if it were held within a limited time frame.

Chinese Society for Social Education Holds Council Meeting

Passes Key Items for This Year's Society Affairs

Facilitating the Implementation of the Ministry-Issued Supplementary Education Plan: The Chinese Society for Social Education held its 16th council meeting on the 25th of this month at the Provincial Education Hall in the capital. Attendees included more than ten directors such as Niu Yongjian, Liang Shuming, Yu Qingtang, Gao Yang, Chen Jianxiao, Chen Lijiang, Ma Zongrong, Gan Yuyuan, and Dong Weichuan. Chen Jianxiao served as chairman, and Ye Dao recorded the minutes. First, Yu Qingtang, the general secretary of the office, reported on the general situation of the society's affairs, the implementation status of the resolutions of the previous council meeting, the latest news on the preparation for the joint establishment of the Guangdong Huaxian Rural Education Experimental Zone, and the process of joining the Chinese Academic Societies Federation. After detailed reports, discussions began. The key items are as follows: (1) Approval of 36 new members. (2) Conducting research on the percentage of illiteracy. (3) Researching the editing and improvement of supplementary reading materials for the public. (4) Promoting the implementation of the Ministry-issued six-year plan for supplementary education for the out-of-school population. As for the date and location of the 5th annual meeting, the standing directors will handle it in full. Furthermore, Ma Zongrong, Chen Jianxiao, Liang Shuming, Zhao Mian, Jiang Wenyu, Zhuang Zexuan, and Meng Xiancheng were appointed to form a central issue committee to draft the central issue for the next annual meeting.
