Fujian Province Conducts Public Education: Over 4.5 Million Out-of-School Adults; Government and Society Jointly Run Public Schools

(Xiamen Correspondence) The Fujian Education Department is implementing supplementary education for out-of-school adults in the province. It has completed a survey of the number of out-of-school adults in various counties and cities in the province who should receive supplementary education. The results are as follows: Provincial capital: 24,906; Changle: 97,060; Minhou: 397,575; numbers for the remaining counties in Eastern and Northern Fujian are omitted; Southwestern Fujian: Tong'an: 855,000; Putian: 17,100; Xianyou: 108,158; Hui'an: 115,425; Jinjiang: 191,375; Nan'an: 171,000; Anxi: 94,050; Jinmen: 18,820; Yongchun: 81,425; Dehua: 43,645; Zhangpu: 89,348; Zhao'an: 45,020; Yunxiao: 50,873; Dongshan: 35,938; Longxi: 138,073; Nanjing: 51,267; Haicheng: 56,003; Pinghe: 60,741; Changtai: 22,230; Longyan: 42,750; Zhangping: 30,353; Ningzhang: 171,000; Datian: 37,620; Yongding: 68,400; Shanghang: 76,950; Hua'an: 21,803; Changting: 71,675; Liancheng: 37,200; Ninghua: 47,025; Mingxi: 16,265; Qingliu: 24,268; Wuping: 52,300; Jianning: 19,992; Xiamen City: 91,442. The total number of people in the province who should receive supplementary education is 4,537,960, which accounts for more than 44% of the province's population of 10,200,000. The key points of the proposed supplementary education center measures are: (1) Implementing the policy of supplementary education for out-of-school adults, focusing on literacy education from the 25th year of the Republic, and gradually shifting to civic education, while also implementing conscript training and self-defense training. (2) Using public schools as the implementing agency, with the curriculum allocating 66% to the national language, 18% to arithmetic, and 8% to music, songs, and physical education. (3) The principle of implementation is to prioritize political power, supplemented by social forces. (4) The method adopted is compulsion, starting with men aged 16 to 35, then extending to women aged 16 to 35, and then to older and younger people. Compulsory enrollment. (5) Each county and city should establish public schools in phases, starting from the 25th year of the Republic, using the Lianbao system as the unit. (6) Large-scale factories and companies should establish a public school starting from the second half of the 25th year of the Republic, specifically to teach out-of-school workers in the factory or company, and close it down when the supplementary education is completed. Public schools will also be established in prisons and the military and police to teach out-of-school prisoners and military and police personnel. Each county's public schools will run two sessions each year, with each session lasting four months. In addition, there are also regulations on teacher training and fundraising. (October 25th)

Letter from the Municipal Health Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau sent a letter stating: "Dear Sir, In the 'Gossip' column of your newspaper on the 23rd of this month, it was stated that 'Luo Ruilan of Liangjiang fell and was injured during the 100-meter preliminary, and was carried to the aid station, where there was no one. The commander's platform shouted, "An athlete is injured, the medical staff should come quickly," and it took a quarter of an hour for someone to arrive slowly, saying "This is not an acute illness."'" It has been found that the medical staff member on duty that day was sent by this bureau. According to the person in question, Ms. Luo was injured while the medical staff member was preparing for a meal. Upon receiving the report, the medical staff member immediately put down their chopsticks and rushed to provide treatment. To reassure the injured person, they told her that the injury was minor and that she should not worry. The medical staff member had neither abandoned their post nor been negligent, and it was also in line with psychological treatment. From both a practical and logical standpoint, there was nothing inappropriate. The news reported in your newspaper is likely based on inaccurate hearsay. We hereby request a correction. Respectfully, Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau. October 27th."

Unified Youth Cultivation (Part 2)

— Ying Guan

(1) Establishing a Conscious Central Concept

This concept is to develop our sound personality. The so-called sound means harmless, evenly developed, harmonious, and complete. The so-called personality includes the physical body, knowledge, skills, behavior, emotions, will, and all aspects of a person's form and spirit. We receive education and training to cultivate and develop a sound personality. All subjects, tasks, and activities are means to achieve this great purpose. It itself is not an end. We must strive for physical education to develop a strong physique, but a strong physique is to cultivate rich knowledge and skills and develop a sound will and character to serve society and humanity. It is not enough to have a strong body to be a player. Every young person should establish such a conscious concept. Then all courses and tasks are for my use, and I am the main body of all work and activities. Although the types of work are numerous, I have a grand purpose and deal with them calmly according to certain steps, not counting success. Why should I be flustered and busy? In the past, educational discussions often divided the scope of activities into three aspects: moral, intellectual, and physical. Later, some advocated adding group education and aesthetic education. In fact, morality is not isolated and must have a group relationship. Aesthetic education cannot be separated from the three aspects of morality, intelligence, and physique. Whether it is the saying of three educations or five educations, there is always a bit of fragmentation and division. Now we should abandon these discussions and only establish a central concept of developing a sound personality in the youth's consciousness, so that their minds can be calm and their spirits concentrated, so that they can study hard and not be scattered, disorganized, confused, and at a loss.

(2) Saving Study Time

With a unified and conscious central concept, the second step is how to save study time. At present, high school students have very little remaining self-study time each day besides class, extracurricular sports, and activities. If we do not pay attention to saving and utilizing it, we will definitely feel more short and insufficient. Many hardworking students get up early to read, reading between classes and after class, before and after meals, and even a few minutes before going to bed, burying themselves in books all day long, practicing the ancient訓 of cherishing every minute. But this method cannot be regarded as truly utilizing time. The real way to utilize time is to first have a limit. Time within the limit should be allocated very reasonably and fully utilized. Time outside the limit should be completely used for rest and play. Rest is static, and play is active. When resting, rest heartily. When playing, play happily. At this time, in addition to maintaining no counter-learning effect, there is absolutely no room for learning. The so-called counter-learning effect means that, for example, we have learned various sheet music in music class according to the fixed solfeggio method. During rest, it is okay to sing arbitrarily to express our feelings, but we cannot arbitrarily change the heights of the tones. Another example is that various hygiene habits have been clarified and familiarized. During rest, there cannot be arbitrary spitting and other situations. We should still maintain various good habits. In short, study time and rest time should be clearly divided. There must be no situation of seeming to study but not studying, seeming to rest but not resting. It is extremely harmful to waste time in a daze. How much is this reasonable time limit? Before there are accurate experimental results to rely on, we have to assume that junior high school and its equivalent schools have eight hours per day, and high school and certain equivalent schools have nine to ten hours per day. As for the largest unit of continuous study time, we can adopt the traditional method of 50 minutes per class. Taking 50 minutes as the limit, after completing 50 minutes of study, there must be a rest of 5 minutes, 10 minutes, or 15 minutes. The total length should be determined according to the complexity of the task. However, there should always be a break in the middle to recover from the fatigue of studying. At present, junior high school students have 31 hours of class per week according to the revised curriculum standards, and the Boy Scout training extracurricular hour is also equal to a regular class, so the total is 32 hours, averaging 5 hours and 20 minutes per day. Calculated in actual time, it is 4 hours and 27 minutes, and the self-study time should be 3 hours and 33 minutes. In addition to the usual 2 hours of self-study in the evening, which actually amounts to 1 hour and 40 minutes, it is necessary to make up for 1 hour and 57 minutes of self-study. Approximately 30 minutes can be used for self-study in the morning, and the remaining 87 minutes must be allocated appropriately in the afternoon. High school students have an average of 9 hours of class per day according to the revised curriculum standards, which actually amounts to 4 hours and 10 minutes. That means there must be 4 hours and 50 minutes or 5 hours and 50 minutes of self-study every day, which is particularly busy. If, due to physical or psychological reasons, you cannot concentrate or feel tired when studying, it is better to reduce the working hours slightly, but the minimum limit cannot be less than 7 hours for junior high school and cannot be less than 8 hours or 8 and a half hours for high school. In addition to having a fixed study scope during class, the allocation of self-study time should be based on the preview and review of each subject, as well as the amount of teaching materials, the difficulty of the content. Each young person should appropriately allocate their own situation. There is one principle to be observed, that is, each subject must strive to achieve the passing standard. If there is remaining energy, read more reference books and do more research work on your favorite subjects. Regarding the allocation of time, it is best to prepare a card every day. From morning to night, record the subject of each study (including class) and the start and end of the time one by one after the study is completed. In this way, you can check the allocation of time for each subject and how much the total study time for the day is still short and should be made up at any time. This is easy to do. Pay attention to it at the beginning, and it will become a habit later. When the allocation of time for each subject and the limit of total study time can be followed from the heart without overstepping the rules, you can no longer need to register. During any kind of study, the most important thing to pay attention to is to concentrate and study attentively. Never let your mind be disturbed and think wildly. Especially in class, a common problem for young people is that they sometimes do not want to listen to unsatisfactory teaching. You must know that learning is for your own use, not responsible to others. You should not let its effect be interrupted, resulting in bad habits that are difficult to correct.

(3) Adopting an Attitude of Only Asking About Cultivation and Not Asking About Harvest

The problem with young people now is not the lack of purpose, but the eagerness to achieve the purpose. Therefore, after having a unified and conscious concept and working hard according to the method of saving time, they are eager to achieve success, often unable to satisfy themselves and feeling bored. They do not know that learning is cumulative, and there is no reason to suddenly get rich. Young people should adopt an attitude of only asking about cultivation and not asking about harvest, set a direction, and steadily build a solid foundation. Then the cultivation of personality can naturally be more than enough on a daily basis, and more than enough on a monthly basis, and more than enough on a yearly basis. (The End)

Team Billiards Championship: Change in Scoring Method

Open Tournament Registration Deadline at the End of the Month

The Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association held its annual meeting at its new venue and elected nine executive committee members for this year: two Chinese and seven Westerners. Old Chairman Mr. Bernal left Shanghai, and Mr. Lie Maijun was publicly elected to succeed him, with Clark as his deputy, Bi Liqu was appointed as honorary secretary, and Packer was appointed as honorary accountant. Since someone is responsible for the association's affairs, the progress of this year's event was continued. Among the resolutions, the most important one was to change the method of determining the victory or defeat of "inter-association" competitions. In the past, the order was determined by the number of wins and losses. Now it is changed to judge the level by the number of points. Each association or team has five players, each with 300 points, totaling 1,500 points. A double round robin system is adopted, meeting each other twice, once in each other's location, to show fairness. The association hopes that the Chinese and Western sports associations and institutions in the city with excellent talents and perfect facilities, such as the Shanghai Banking Club, the French Chamber of Commerce, the Western Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese YMCA, the Western Overseas YMCA, the International Sports Association, and the Portuguese General Association, will participate in the cooperation. As for other advanced and primary open tournaments and the Slacker tournament, the registration deadline is still set at the end of this month, and the competition will start on the 16th of next month.

Recent Overview of Soviet Russian Sports

— Song Ruhai

The Soviet Russian Federation is indeed a country worthy of the most attention from all countries in the world today. Since the revolution in 1917, only 19 years have passed, and in these 19 years, the rapid progress and effectiveness of social, economic, cultural, and political advancements are truly amazing in human history, surpassing any country in the world. Now, the people of the whole country are all inspired by the enthusiasm of "creating a new world," and everyone is working hard to move forward and catch up, participating in the so-called "communist socialist activities" with one heart. Before the revolution, everyone knew that Russia was the most backward nation in Europe. The unsound organization of the state and society, the lack of education, the underdeveloped science, the demoralized people, the superstition of ghosts and gods, class struggle, and racial conflict were all countless, which was the cause of the revolution. However, after the revolution, Soviet Russia suddenly jumped from an agricultural society to an industrial society. Not to mention other things, just in terms of the railway lines in the country, they have now reached all parts of the country. In addition, the most striking thing is the great factories in various cities, towering into the clouds, standing side by side, and their architectural styles are all constructed according to the latest scientific methods. Secondly, the lives of farmers have also been greatly improved. Four-fifths of the country's farmers have organized rural cooperatives, and the rest are engaged in imitation. There are currently more than 385,500 agricultural machines in rural areas. In addition, the Soviet Russian Arctic icebreaker sails on Arctic expeditions every winter, about several times. Especially for training aircraft pilots, every big city has training centers. About 100,000 ordinary people participate in skydiving on airplanes. This is to practice for future foreign aggression. These people can use airplanes to invade enemy territory and disrupt the enemy's rear. This kind of sport is now the most effort in European countries and is the only trend of the newest type of warfare. Also, the Soviet Russian railway line goes directly to Central Asia, deep into the barren land, and wants to use the latest agricultural machinery and electricity in no man's land to cultivate this kind of wilderness and establish state-owned collective farms. During this process of rapid transformation, the Soviet Union not only focuses on the increase in material quantity, but also constantly seeks to transform the purpose of life, psychological construction, family organization, marriage of men and women, social education, and other issues.

During the era of the Russian Tsar, the authority of the empire was used to control small and weak nations. There were about 189 kinds of such nations within Russia. At that time, all of them were regarded as slaves and concubines, but after the revolution, all the small and weak nations were regarded as equal citizens by the Soviet Russian Federation. Now, men and women of all ethnic groups enjoy equal education. They also have the right to vote and be elected in politics. Moreover, the central government uses the languages of various states to publish daily newspapers, establish schools, public theaters, etc. In Central Asia, more than 11,000 public schools and more than 300 kinds of daily newspapers have been established, paying special attention to social education. Children's production registration offices, public childcare bureaus, parks, public sports fields, swimming pools, skating rinks, dance halls, music halls, workers' clubs, children's parks, young pioneer camps, etc. are set up in urban areas. Major railway stations have set up child custody offices. Women traveling with children, from swaddling clothes to eight years old, can be entrusted to them for a period of time from six hours to two days. Therefore, all mothers find it extremely convenient. All the facilities for serving social work are available. Speaking of the Soviet Russian territory, it accounts for one-sixth of the world's area, with more than 8 million square miles of land and a population of about 170 million, with as many as 189 kinds of races. It is admirable to be able to cooperate and jointly organize this new type of communist society. Let us describe the current situation of sports development from this brief historical background.

Soviet Russian leader Stalin often used sincere words to say to the people in his speeches: "The human body structure is a kind of generative machine. We should pay special attention to making this machine sound in its entirety, and then we can manage and use various mechanical machines made by human hands." Indeed, the Soviet Russian five-year plan is not only amazing in the development of social economy, industry, and agriculture, but also shows amazing results in social education and public sports. Under this new system, the output of factories, farms, and mining areas has increased several times. The level of national education, scientific common sense, and worker skills have also been greatly improved. Men and women of all classes in the country do their best to produce and do their best to rush to create the supply of materials, so that each individual can jointly enjoy the happiness of materials. In 1939, the labor world produced a new type of movement called Stakhanorite. This movement is popular in factories, rural areas, mining areas, government agencies, education circles, etc. across the country. Stakhanorite is a worker in a coal mining area. He worked especially hard in his mining work. His daily output was more than double that of the workers in the entire mining area. Therefore, the labor world used his working speed as a model and initiated this movement to promote the speed of working time and expand the output of factories and farmland. Since this linkage was initiated, in less than two years, the national workers and farmers have been working hard to move forward and catch up. Each person has worked diligently and diligently to get this honorable title. If a worker gets this title, the wages will also be doubled. Ordinary workers only earn 150 rubles per day (each ruble is equal to 1.3 yuan in national currency). If they get this title, their monthly salary can be increased to 500 to 1,000 rubles. Since the generation record of this movement, the special skills of the labor world have increased by thousands of people every year, and the output of workers, farmers, and mines has doubled every year. People's lives have therefore improved. During this economic development, the authorities believe that promoting people's health is an indispensable way.

The Soviet Union established the Central Supreme Sports Committee (Svpreme Council for Phyoical Tcainino) in 1930, and established branches in various cities, factories, mining areas, collective farms, railway lines, troops, and agencies. The facilities for physical education are planned strictly. The sports branch in each place reports its methods and results to the Central Sports Committee at the end of each semester. The central government also stipulates an Efficiency Test called B.G.T.O. (Beadvfor Labour and Defence) for boys and girls from 14 to 16 years old, and the second is called Readv for Laboor andDefence.e G.T O. for young men and women over 16 years old. Chairman Ma Lin of Qinghai Provincial Government Sets Sail to Mecca for Pilgrimage

Received 10,000 Yuan for Travel Expenses from President Chiang

According to the Central News Agency, Chairman Ma Lin of Qinghai Provincial Government visited Mayor Wu and Commander of the Songhu Garrison Yang Hu yesterday morning to bid farewell. At noon, he and his two sons, Bu Yuan and A Heng, Ma Zhengqing, Ma Li, and eleven followers departed from the Xinguang Wharf by the Hong Kong ferry to cross the river to the Blue Funnel Wharf. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, they boarded the Blue Funnel Line's Aphilon and set sail, leaving Shanghai to go abroad. Among those traveling together were 126 Muslims from provinces such as Qinghai and Gansu, and Ma Qishan, the 15th Route Army Corps Commander. Chairman Ma and his group will first go to Singapore, then transfer to another ship to Jeddah, and then land and travel overland to Mecca for pilgrimage. Chairman Ma will travel to various parts of Arabia after the pilgrimage and is scheduled to return to China in mid-March next year.

Farewell Party

Those who went to the ship to say goodbye yesterday afternoon included Tang Guozhen, representative of Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Northwest Bandit Suppression Zhang Xueliang; Li Dachao, representative of Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Yang Hu, Commander of the Songhu Garrison; Du Yuesheng; Tan Kemin, member and Secretary-General of the Qinghai Provincial Government; Central Committee member Tian Kunshan; Chen Guangzhong, representative of Cai Jinjun, Director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau; the wife of Zhu Shaoliang, Director of the Gansu Pacification Office, as well as many relatives, friends, and subordinates of Chairman Ma.

Chiang's Travel Expenses Gift

After Chairman Ma leaves the country, the position of Chairman of the Qinghai Provincial Government will be taken over by Ma Bufang, Ma's nephew and member of the Qinghai Provincial Government. Chairman Ma recently went to Beijing to meet with President Chiang and requested an extension of his original six-month leave by five months, which was approved by President Chiang. President Chiang also gave Ma 10,000 yuan for travel expenses, which was handed over to Tan Kemin, member and Secretary-General of the Qinghai Provincial Government, to be forwarded. Ma has already telegraphed his gratitude to President Chiang for his preferential treatment of border personnel.

Ma's Remarks

Chairman Ma said in an interview on the ship before his departure, "I am going abroad to Mecca for pilgrimage this time, and the trip will take about four months. I am scheduled to return to China in mid-March next year. During my absence, Ma Bufang will act as chairman of Qinghai Province. My previous visit to Beijing was very good, and I am especially grateful and excited for the preferential treatment given to border personnel by President Chiang and the central authorities. However, due to the short time in Beijing, I did not have the opportunity to visit the capital's agencies and construction projects, so I plan to stay in Beijing for a while after returning to China next year to visit in detail before returning to Qinghai to preside over the provincial government."

Tan Returns to Qinghai Immediately

Tan Kemin, member and Secretary-General of the Qinghai Provincial Government, accompanied Chairman Ma to Beijing this time to report to the central government on provincial affairs and came to Shanghai to bid farewell to Chairman Ma before his departure. He plans to stay in Shanghai for a day or two before returning to Qinghai to take up his duties.

Yesterday Was U.S. Navy Day; U.S. Warship Sailors Stationed in Shanghai Given Leave to Go Ashore for Entertainment

Yesterday was U.S. Navy Day. Sailors from the seventeen U.S. warships docked in the port were given leave to go ashore for entertainment. Therefore, many entertainment venues, cafes, and bars were filled with U.S. sailors. This holiday began in 1922 and was initiated by the U.S. Navy League. Since then, celebrations have been held every year on this day. The reason for choosing October 27 is that it is the birthday of Roosevelt. As Assistant Secretary of the Navy and President, Roosevelt promoted the Navy with all his might, so it is used to commemorate his achievements. On October 1775, the U.S. Congress also passed a bill on this day to allocate US$100,000 to create the Navy and appointed a committee to purchase warships. Twenty-three years later, the Department of the Navy was established and gradually expanded the Navy. Today, the U.S. Navy has become one of the most powerful in the world.

Today is Czech National Day; Czech Nationals Hold Celebrations

Today is the 18th anniversary of the founding of the Czechoslovak Republic. Czech nationals all over the world are holding celebrations on this day. The Czech Embassy and Czech nationals in this port are also holding celebrations. The territory of the Czech Republic was originally part of the Austro-Hungarian Empire. During the European War, the Czech people openly rebelled against the Habsburg Dynasty. Czech prisoners of war in Russia formed the Czech Foreign Legion and fought on the Russian side, galloping across Siberia, occupying the railway that crossed the area, and advancing to Vladivostok to return home to advocate independence. At that time, Czech soldiers in the Austrian army on various fronts fled to the Allied forces and formed independent armies, establishing great military achievements. Their political leaders, Professor Masaryk and Dr. Beneš, also fled abroad to fight tirelessly for the liberation of the Czech nation. As a result, after losing independence and freedom for three hundred years, they were able to announce the establishment of the Republic in Prague on October 28, 1918. Its first president was Professor Masaryk. After taking office, he worked hard to govern the country, and the country's fortunes continued to rise until 1935, when Dr. Beneš was re-elected as his successor. From the day the country was founded to the day he took office as president, he was in charge of diplomacy, and his political achievements were admired by people all over Europe. Czech foreign policy aims to maintain peace in Central Europe and to cooperate with member states of the League of Nations. Therefore, it formed the Little Entente with Yugoslavia and Romania. In the past ten years, this alliance has been the main factor in maintaining peace in Central Europe. Later, the Little Entente revived Greece and Turkey and established the Balkan Pact to maintain peace in southeastern Europe. The Czech Republic's peaceful policy and that of the Little Entente always complemented France's peaceful policy. This year, the Czech Republic revived cooperation with the Soviet Union, and European peace has gained another layer of security. Although the Czech Republic has been established for eighteen years, its domestic industry and commerce have developed rapidly, and its economy and finance have become increasingly consolidated. In these eighteen years, there have been no internal conflicts in the country, making it a very peaceful place in Central Europe. And at a time when dictatorships are prevalent today, the Czech Republic still maintains its democratic parliamentary system, which is a special feature.

The Minyuan Steamer Ran Aground Midway; It Escaped Danger and Went to Yichang; Passenger Li Denghui Transferred to Minfeng to Go to Sichuan

The Minsheng Industrial Company commissioned the Jiangnan Shipyard to build two sister ships, Minben and Minyuan. After completion, they were dedicated to the Shanghai-Chongqing route. The gross tonnage of the ship is 1,500 tons, and the net tonnage is 600 tons. On the 21st of this month, it loaded cargo and passengers in Shanghai and sailed to Chongqing. At 5:00 PM on the 25th, it sailed to the Yidu County section of the Yangtze River above Hankou and below Yichang. Because the river water was very shallow in this section, the ship's draft reached nine and a half feet, which caused it to run aground. The shipowner tried to rescue it without success, and immediately reported to the general and branch offices in Chongqing, Yichang, Hankou, and Shanghai by radio. After receiving the telegram, the Yichang branch office sent a ship to rescue it. Coincidentally, the Minfeng ship of the company's Shenyu Line, which was sailing from Shanghai to Chongqing, passed the grounding site of the Minyuan. It transferred passengers, including Li Denghui, the former president of Fudan University in Shanghai, to the ship, and continued to sail to Chongqing as usual. The ship sent by Yichang to rescue it has arrived and unloaded the cotton yarn and cloth that the Minyuan was carrying in order to reduce the draft. It is expected to be able to escape danger after the tide rises.

The Shanghai Minsheng Company received a radio report from the Minyuan ship yesterday stating that it had floated out of the shallows and was sailing to Yichang.

Gao Hanqian Returns from European Inspection Tour, Discussing Wartime Finance and Controlled Economy, Departs for Japan Again Yesterday for Further Investigation

A Central News Agency report states that Mr. Gao Hanqian, formerly dispatched by the Fujian Provincial Government to various European countries to study political economy, has now completed his mission and returned to China, residing at the East Asia Hotel. The reporter, recognizing Mr. Gao's many years of experience in finance, believed that his return from this inspection tour must have yielded valuable insights, and therefore sought an interview. Mr. Gao responded that he had visited over ten European countries and received the care of the embassies, which greatly facilitated the collection of materials for his studies. However, political economy is a vast field, and he initially planned to focus on: 1. Wartime finance, 2. Controlled resources, 3. Management of production enterprises. These three items are also quite complex, and due to time constraints, he would only provide a brief overview.

All countries are preparing for wartime finance with increasing intensity. Many countries have experience from the First World War, making it easier to proceed. Regarding the tax system, indirect taxes are fluid and likely to be greatly affected during wartime. More stable direct taxes, such as income tax and inheritance tax, should be implemented. After the outbreak of war, wartime public bonds can be raised and wartime paper money issued. Securities with foreign value should be collected; Germany advocates nationalizing these securities, while Britain and France advocate that national banks purchase them at market value.

The Netherlands has comprehensive management of production enterprises. Since 1929, the world has been in recession, but the Netherlands restricts imports and exports of goods from stores, basing them on the amount in 1928. Any excess is temporarily stored in warehouses. For example, if a family raises five cows and ten sows, they are allowed to keep one calf and two piglets from the next year's production. Any excess can be distributed by the government as food for the unemployed and impoverished. These are just a few examples to illustrate the rest.

Italy's controlled economy is particularly well-planned. Since 1923, when Mussolini came to power, he observed that countries were supporting laborers by organizing unions, while also protecting capitalists and allowing them to shut down freely. This resulted in labor-capital confrontation, mutual loss, and plunging the social economy into an irrecoverable state. Mussolini first declared that workers' strikes and employers' free factory closures were strictly prohibited. Laws were enacted to organize labor-capital industry groups, with a central labor-capital mutual aid department, headed by Mussolini himself. Under the department, there was a national labor-capital mutual aid conference, composed of nine major industry associations, twenty-two labor-capital mutual aid societies, a standing executive committee, and a resident expert committee. Most committee members were representatives elected by county industry associations to participate in provincial industry federations, and representatives from provincial federations participated in national industry federations. Representatives from the national federation then attended the national conference of the labor-capital mutual aid department.

First, in terms of labor-capital adjustment, cooperative and mutual aid groups are integrated, preventing conflict and promoting coexistence and prosperity, achieving the effect of sharing the same boat. Second, in terms of adjusting statistics, systematic and organized groups report sequentially from county to province to nation, comprehensively and completely, without any omissions. Third, in terms of a controlled economy, the quantity of agricultural production is based on the needs of factory manufacturing and the limits of commodity sales, using commerce to control industry and industry to control agriculture, eliminating the concern of overproduction. Moreover, the government can concentrate a certain amount of manpower, financial resources, and material resources within a certain period for internal administration or external warfare, with prior calculations leading to successful outcomes, which is natural.

It is reported that Mr. Gao took the President Jefferson again yesterday to Japan for investigation, so as to complete the mission.

Reduced Stamp Tax, Order to Step Up Supervision, Tax Office Transmits Orders to Supervisors

According to Da Gong News Agency, the Ministry of Finance telegraphed the stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus of each province and city, and the stamp tax commissioners, ordering them as follows: "Since the reform of the stamp tax last year, the monthly tax revenue has been stipulated to be allocated to local areas to reduce land tax surcharges and eliminate harsh miscellaneous taxes. Therefore, the surplus or deficit of tax revenue greatly affects the central treasury revenue and the allocation to local areas. Recently, after reading the post office reports, since March of this year, the number of stamps sold by post offices in various provinces and cities is mostly smaller than the revenue in the same month last year. The reason for this is undoubtedly due to lax enforcement of inspections. In order to eliminate concealment, increase tax revenue, and maintain the income of the national and local treasuries, inspections and spot checks should be stepped up. In addition to separate telegrams, we hereby request that you check and instruct all inspectors to comply accordingly." It is reported that after receiving the order, the Tax Administration has already distributed it to the supervisory commissioners to step up inspections in various places in order to maintain tax revenue.

Pan Xulun Lectures on Income Tax, Factories and Shops Should Prepare, Lectures at the Knitting Industry Association Yesterday, Revise Bookkeeping and Register Capital

The Shanghai Knitting Industry Association has more than 140 member manufacturers. For the purpose of studying the implementation of income tax, an income tax research committee has been organized. Yesterday, a meeting was held at Yizhixiang on Simalu Road, inviting Mr. Pan Xulun, director and accountant of the Lixin Accounting Firm, to give a lecture on "Preparations that Manufacturers Should Urgently Make Before the Implementation of Income Tax." Attendees included Yu Tinghui, chairman of the association, Cai Yinqiao, owner of China First Knitting Factory, Zheng Hairuo, general manager of Xinsheng Manufacturing Factory, Ge Shengru, owner of Qiuzhi Knitting Factory, and dozens of others. Excerpts from Mr. Pan's speech are as follows:

The profit portion of income tax in our country should start being taxed from January 1st next year, which is very soon. All manufacturers should prepare early to avoid being caught off guard. According to the current situation of manufacturers, there are three things that should be prepared immediately:

(1) Improve incomplete bookkeeping and establish accurate bookkeeping. Most knitting factories are sole proprietorships or partnerships, and most are small in scale. Because the managers are mostly shop owners, or closely related to shop owners, they trust each other on weekdays, so they do not pay much attention to bookkeeping, and some even lack records. Now, because income tax must be paid, accurate bookkeeping is necessary to calculate accurate profits and losses and provide reliable evidence. Only then can taxes be paid accordingly to avoid trouble. If there is no accurate bookkeeping, the amount of income can only be estimated. Overestimating will result in paying excessive taxes, while underestimating will result in tax evasion. Moreover, if the manufacturer itself cannot provide accurate accounts to prove the correctness of its income calculation, then the tax officials can legally estimate the amount of tax to be paid, and the taxpayer can only endure it without objection. Therefore, improving bookkeeping is currently the most important task for all factories and shops and should not be delayed any longer. To help all factories improve accounting, the association can organize bookkeeping training classes, inviting factories to send bookkeepers to attend lectures and practice. The teaching should focus on bookkeeping and accounting systems applicable to the industry. In this way, factories can improve bookkeeping without changing personnel in a short period of time.

(2) Quickly estimate the amount of capital and apply for registration or apply for a change of registration. The capital amount of factories and shops that are sole proprietorships or partnerships is not fixed. However, in general, the capital amount recorded on the books of each factory and shop is often very small, while the annual business volume is many times or dozens of times greater than its capital amount. The source of funds is that the owners or partners raise funds on behalf of themselves, or borrow them themselves, without treating them as capital, or save undistributed profits as public accumulation, or withdraw secret public funds every year. Therefore, the capital amount on the books is only a nominal amount without actual substance. If this nominal capital amount is used as the standard for calculating the income ratio, then the factory will suffer unnecessary tax losses, which is unnecessary. Therefore, the first step is for each factory to quickly recalculate its capital amount. All public accumulation and secret public accumulation should be appropriately converted into capital. Even funds that are lent to the business by the shareholders themselves and have a long-term nature should also be converted into capital. In this way, the calculation of the income ratio will be accurate, and paying taxes according to the legal progressive rate will not be disadvantageous. However, the determination of the capital amount should be based on those who have been approved for registration by the competent authorities. In the past, business registration was not widespread. The capital amount was noted on the registration documents and was originally a statistical matter, which was insignificant. Now that the capital amount has become the basis for calculating the tax amount, all factories and shops that have not been approved for registration should immediately apply to the local competent authorities for approval of registration and request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to issue a license. In the event of taxation, the capital amount can be avoided without unnecessary disputes. If it is not registered, the capital of the manufacturer cannot be determined, and the tax collector may need to check his accounts at any time, which will cause a lot of trouble and is not appropriate. As for factories and shops that have already been approved for registration, their capital amount is also often inaccurate and should be recalculated immediately, that is, apply for a registration change of capital. Regarding this point, the report stated that the Ministry of Finance has requested the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to quickly revise the commercial registration rules and order merchants to comply with them. Therefore, when applying for business registration in the future, the competent authorities will have strict inspections of the capital of the business to prevent abuse of reporting. All businesses must pay attention and apply early. As for domestic industrial and commercial organizations with a corporate structure, most have already been registered, and their capital amount is mostly fixed. However, those who should apply for registration of increased capital should also pay attention to handling it as soon as possible.

In addition to the above two points, there are many other matters that factories and shops should pay attention to and study before the implementation of income tax. However, none is as urgent as the above two, so they are specifically mentioned to promote everyone's attention.

Electrical Silk Weaving Industry Holds, Certificate of Silk Weaving Stamped

In order to assist the government in cracking down on smuggling and to maintain the sales of legitimate goods, the Shanghai Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association began on the 1st of this month to conduct silk fabric identification, stamping the ends of silk fabrics produced by members to prove their authenticity and facilitate sales. The association's official letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce is recorded below:

"To whom it may concern, in order to assist the government in cracking down on smuggling and to maintain the sales of legitimate goods, our association began on October 1st to conduct silk fabric identification for members, stamping the ends of silk fabrics to prove their authenticity. Currently, all products of members, whether old or new, are being stamped at the same time, with the aim of completing all procedures before October 30th, so that from November 1st, all silk fabrics produced by members will have the stamp of our association to prove their authenticity. If silk fabrics are not stamped, they have not undergone identification procedures, and our association will no longer certify them. In this way, for members' products transported to the interior, when encountering anti-smuggling agencies along the way, they can easily identify them at both ends of the silk fabrics, so that legitimate domestic products can have the opportunity to facilitate sales. In addition to submitting two copies of our association's silk fabric identification rules, we hereby submit two copies of the seal used to stamp the ends of silk fabrics for your reference. We kindly request that you forward it to the Ministry of Finance to notify the anti-smuggling agencies in each province and city to verify this seal when inspecting products from Shanghai silk weaving factories, and to release them along with the transportation or distribution license, so as to prove their authenticity and facilitate sales. We respectfully thank you for your public spirit."

Miserable situation, find ways to send them back

In Russia

Two more overseas Chinese residing in Vladivostok, Soviet Union, who were deported back to China by the Soviet authorities due to old age and unemployment, arrived in Shanghai on the Russian ship North. The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau sent personnel to inquire about their situation and extracted their names, ages, and places of origin as follows: (1) Tao Xingxi, 56 years old, from Penglai County, Shandong Province, has lived in Vladivostok for 25 years; (2) Fang Xishan, 67 years old, from Laiyang County, Donglai, has lived in Vladivostok for 32 years. Both were laborers.

In Japan

Four overseas Chinese from Japan: (1) Wu Ti kuan, 41 years old; (2) Jiang Mingzhai, 33 years old; (3) Zhu Genpeng, 31 years old; (4) Zheng Suishi, 35 years old. The above four people are all from Qingtian County, Zhejiang Province. They were coal pickers in Tokyo. They have lived in Japan for as long as 13 years and as little as seven or eight years. They were deported one after another and arrived in Shanghai on the Rokkomaru, in extremely miserable circumstances.

In the Philippines

Dong Guanghai, a 21-year-old overseas Chinese from Quanzhou, Fujian Province, who resided in the Philippines, has been doing business in the Philippines for many years. He has also been affected by the recession in the Nanyang Islands and is unable to make a living, so he returned to China to Shanghai in dismay. The above overseas Chinese have been separated by the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau according to their places of origin and have been helped to obtain ship tickets to send them back to their original places of origin.

Chen Guirong's Ear Injury Case

Intended to Steal, Twisted His Left Ear

According to a report in the Chinese-American Evening Post on the 17th of this month, a man from Nanxun named Chen Guirong was stabbed in the left ear by Japanese soldiers. Some people have distributed leaflets to express their indignation. In order to clarify the truth of the case, the reporter has made many inquiries. The results of the investigation by the Public Concession and the Public Security Bureau reveal that the reason for the injury to Chen Guirong's ear was that the man sneaked into a house in Zhabei with the intention of stealing. Fearing that the truth about the injury would be revealed to the hospital, he would be detained and fined by the police, so he fabricated a story to avoid punishment. The hospital then reported the information to the police station, resulting in a miscommunication. After investigation, it was all fiction, and it was found that the man was a habitual offender, and stealing was not the first time. His arm was tattooed with criminal marks.

Ministry of Finance Formulates Penalties for Mineral Products

The Ministry of Finance yesterday issued instructions to all tax bureaus and tax management offices regarding the handling of violations of mineral products: "After investigating violations of mineral products, regarding the review method, the most recent announcement, the temporary regulations on the review of violations by each district tax bureau and each sub-district tax management office, can be used as a basis. As for the rules on punishment, before the regulations on the punishment of mineral products are formulated, those who seriously conceal tax evasion may be punished in accordance with the provisions of Article 116 of the Mining Law, in addition to tax supplementation, a fine of more than one time to five times the amount of tax payable shall be imposed. Those with minor circumstances, or non-compliance with procedures, or unreported inspection, and no tax evasion, should be handled in accordance with the punishment regulations of other unified taxes. The amount of punishment shall not exceed twice the amount of tax payable (abbreviated below)."

Yeh Fu-kang Accused: The Facts Are Entirely Fabricated

Four Lawyers' Statement: Lawyers Ren Wei, Cai Ding, Gu Ao, and Shen Zengkuan state: In May of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, Wang Hanqing commissioned us lawyers to act on his behalf in filing a private prosecution with the Shanghai First Special District Court against Yeh Fu-kang for financial fraud. Yeh Fu-kang went to the lawyers' office and invited Wang Hanqing to explain the matter in person, and a petition was submitted requesting permission to withdraw the private prosecution. Recently, we have read in various Shanghai newspapers that Yeh Fu-kang incited theft of gold bars and seduced Wang Hanqing's wife, and that Wang Hanqing was sentenced to one year and six months in prison, with the case delayed for two or three years due to appeals. Yeh, taking advantage of Wang's wife's youth, seduced her into adultery, and so on. Upon investigation, the case against the person involved, Wang Hanxiang, previously prosecuted by the Hongkou police, was declared not guilty by the Shanghai First Special District Court in a criminal judgment on May 28th of the 20th year of the Republic of China. As for the private prosecution case, Wang Hanqing was not involved in the theft of gold bars, and Yeh Fu-kang did not incite the theft of gold bars. Wang Hanqing was never sentenced to one year and six months in prison and detained for two or three years, and Yeh Fu-kang did not take advantage of the opportunity to seduce Wang's wife. The original case file is available for review. The reports in the newspapers are inevitably inaccurate due to hearsay. We are deeply concerned that this will confuse public opinion, and we hereby issue this statement on October 26th of the 25th year of the Republic of China.

Yeh Fu-kang's Letter: To the Editor, Your newspaper published a news item on the 25th of this month concerning accusations against me. Not only is it completely inconsistent with the facts, but it is also full of malicious libel and defamation. My former lawyer representing Wang Hanqing, Gu Ao, Cha Renwei, Cai Ding, Shen Zengkuan, and others, have issued a statement in today's Shen Bao and Xin Bao newspapers clarifying everything. Now, I select the most outrageous fabricated facts and list them as follows: 1. In the Republic of China's year of X, Wang Hanqing was arrested for theft and appointed me for defense. He was declared not guilty in the initial trial. In the Republic of China's year of X+2, Wang Hanqing falsely accused me of defrauding him of public funds, but later, realizing his case was unfounded and fearing false accusation, he withdrew the private prosecution, as certified by lawyers Gu Ao, Cha Renwei, Cai Ding, Shen Zengkuan, and others. This can be verified in case file number 704 of the First Special District Court of the Republic of China's year of X+1. 2. Wang Hanqing's theft case and private prosecution case do not involve any gold bars (all can be verified in court files). However, someone has fabricated shocking rumors about inciting the theft of gold bars and sharing the gold bars. 3. Wang Hanqing's theft case resulted in an acquittal in the initial trial, and he returned to Hankou with Wang Zhangshi. How could there be a sentence of one year and six months in prison, and how could there be an opportunity to seduce an old woman nearing fifty with a cormorant-like face by delaying detention through appeals? (All of this can be verified in court files.) 4. The "Little Luzon Hat Shop" was acquired in the Republic of China's year of X-1 (there is a transfer certificate from the Spanish consulate that can be verified). Wang Hanqing appointed me as his defense attorney around May or June of the Republic of China's year of X. However, it is falsely claimed that I defrauded him of funds to open the shop. Other fabrications, such as the Ministry of Justice sending personnel and various judicial absurdities, are nothing more than shocking and outrageous statements for other purposes. Because the case is under investigation, I must maintain confidentiality, and I, Fu-kang, do not want to say more. However, Wang Hanqing believes I am weak and can be bullied, and has spoken such nonsense. Even a just newspaper like yours has been misled, causing society to laugh and relatives and friends to be horrified. I have no choice but to state the facts and respectfully request a correction. To the Shen Bao Newspaper, Yeh Fu-kang.

Attention: Road Traffic Safety

The Bureau of Public Works Ordered to Forward Instructions to Transportation Companies, etc., for Information.

The National Highway Traffic Commission, considering that the intersection of railroads and highways is most prone to danger, has resolved three measures for the sake of safety: (1) Request the Ministry of Railways to install barriers at intersections of railways and highways where barriers have not yet been installed. (2) Send letters to provinces and cities to erect train warning signs on highways. (3) Send letters to provinces and cities instructing highway traffic authorities to order vehicles or livestock crossing railroads without barriers to proceed according to the following steps, regardless of whether a train is approaching: (A) Stop at a safe distance from the railroad. (B) Look clearly along the railroad in both directions for trains. (C) Listen for the sound of approaching trains. (D) If a train is seen or heard approaching, wait at the original stopping point until the train has passed before crossing. (E) Only cross if no train is approaching. It is now learned that the establishment of barriers and traffic signs has been requested by the Secretariat of the National Economic Commission to the Ministry of Railways and the competent authorities of various provinces and cities. The Shanghai Municipal Government has approved the Secretariat's letter regarding the third measure and has instructed the Municipal Bureau of Public Works to forward it to the city's long-distance bus companies, taxi trade associations, freight truck trade associations, and automobile firms for information.

Lawyer Bao Gang Accused of Seduction Case Involves the Chief of Chuansha District Office. Supervisory Department Sends Personnel to Court to Interrogate Zhang Qinghong. The Case is Serious, Bao Gang Posts an Additional 3,000 Yuan Bail.

Lawyer Bao Gang has been accused by Cui Changgui, a chauffeur from the Special Affairs Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and his fiancée Yang Yuehua. Although Yang Yuehua and Cui Changgui are not married, they have been living together. After a quarrel, Zhang Xingu, a servant from Bao Gang's office, took her to Bao's office and incited her to divorce. She was then defiled by Bao at the Dafang Hotel. When Cui reported the matter to the Detective Team, Bao hid Yang Yuehua in the countryside of Pudong. They requested an investigation. Prosecutor Kong of the District Court has filed a public prosecution against Bao and Zhang Xingu for the crime of

hindering family happiness

After repeated examinations, Bao claimed it was a conspiracy to extort money. Yesterday morning, Judge Xie Zhengnong opened the Fourth Criminal Court for trial. According to Cui Changgui's testimony, he is 27 years old, from Shandong, and became engaged to Yang Yuehua on February 14th of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. They had not married because his mother died. They began living together on July 17th of the 23rd year. He used to live in the same lane as Bao Gang, Bao lived at number 4, and he lived at number 9. On the morning of May 10th of this year, he quarreled with his wife, and friends advised them to separate. He did not know that his wife had gone out or about Bao Gang and others. He reported to the bureau after his wife had not returned since May 17th and he

could not find her anywhere

Later, a friend told him she was in Pudong. He went and found his wife, but Bao Gang was not there. As for the witness Zhou Mingxuan, a tea server at the Dafang Hotel, he testified, "I have never seen Yang Yuehua, nor do I recognize her. As for who came to open the room, I don't remember clearly." Then, the witness Zhang Qinghong, the chief of the Third District of Chuansha County, testified that he did not know Bao Gang, nor had Yang Yuehua ever been to his office. The judge ordered Zhang to sit in the audience, and ordered Yang Yuehua to testify in court. Yang Yuehua claimed that when Bao Gang took her to the countryside, she had been to the Third District Office of Chuansha, which was located at

Gongjia Road Intersection

and met the District Chief Zhang Qinghong. The judge said, "Then if you saw the District Chief, you must recognize him." She replied, "I recognize him." The judge ordered her to look closely among the audience to see if he was there. Yang Yuehua pointed out Zhang Qinghong. The judge immediately questioned him why he claimed he had never seen her. Zhang replied, "As the Chief of the Third District, there are 100,000 people in that area. How could anyone not recognize me?" By this time, it was almost noon. The presiding judge then declared that the case was being investigated by the Supervisory Committee on the orders of the President of the Court, and the situation was relatively serious. Bao Gang should post an additional 3,000 yuan in bail, and Zhang Xingu should post an additional 1,000 yuan in bail. All

witnesses and evidence

should be brought to the court at 1:30 PM for further questioning and to await the investigator from the Supervisory Committee. The court was then adjourned. In the afternoon, after all the witnesses arrived, Wu Zhang (Zi Zhuochen, from Hunan), the secretary and chief of the General Affairs Section dispatched by the Jiangsu Supervisory District Commissioner's Office, opened the hearing in the First Criminal Court. Initially, after Bao Gang was accused, the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau arrested Bao's wife, but she was released after being sent to the District Court. Bao's wife then accused the former Detective Team Leader Zhang Datong and others of dereliction of duty at the Supervisory Yuan. The Jiangsu Supervisory Commissioner's Office issued an order to investigate. When the committee member came to Shanghai, he first went to the Public Security Bureau to investigate. The Public Security Bureau informed him that Zhang Datong had already been

dismissed from his post

However, the bureau's opinion was that Zhang Qinghong, the Chief of the Third District of Chuansha County, was also guilty of hiding the seduced person on behalf of Bao Gang. Therefore, the bureau accused Zhang of illegality and requested a joint investigation. Therefore, after the supervisory committee member arrived at the court, he first focused on Zhang Qinghong's matter. After the hearing began, he first questioned Cui Changgui and Yang Yuehua, whose testimonies were the same as before. Yang Yuehua also claimed that she had lived in Zhang Qinghong's house for many days and had taken photos with Zhang's concubine. Then Cui Changgui was asked, "You said that when Bao Gang abducted Yang Yuehua, he took 360 yuan. Do you

have any evidence to the contrary

He replied, "Yes, I won the lottery and borrowed money from Director Liu, both of whom can testify." Then, he asked Yang Yuehua, "Have you gotten the property back?" She replied, "I only got back a watch and a ring, the rest I haven't gotten back." Then, he questioned Zhang Qinghong, 32 years old, from Chuansha, a graduate of Pudong Middle School, who has been the Chief of the Third District of Chuansha County since he was 25 years old. He is very strict with himself and has no relationship with either party. He asked, "Do you often come to Shanghai?" He replied, "Once or twice a month, to purchase things for the office in Shanghai." He asked, "Do you know about Bao Gang's matter?" He replied, "I don't know." The supervisory committee member then stated, "I came here because Bao Gang's wife

went to the Supervisory Yuan

to accuse the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau of dereliction of duty, indiscriminately detaining and torturing innocent people. You are a district chief and a person who knows the law. Why did you hide the criminal? You should explain the whole situation." He replied, "Yang Yuehua has never been to my office." He asked, "Bao Gang is your fellow villager and good friend. He is taking a concubine. He stayed at your house for two days. You don't know the situation? It is also common courtesy. You should know that if you knowingly concealed it, you are a civil servant and not only violated the criminal law, the Supervisory Yuan should also impeach you." He replied, "I request that the superiors investigate in Chuansha County. If I have indeed concealed the fugitive Yang Yuehua, I am willing to receive the most

severe punishment

He asked, "I have never been to Chuansha. How is your character? I don't know. But can the County Chief of Chuansha County and the chiefs of the other districts in the county guarantee that you would never do this?" He replied, "Yes, they can." He asked, "Can you ask your county chief to investigate?" He replied, "I don't have this authority. I can make a written statement and ask the Supervisory Yuan to send a letter to the County Chief to investigate." At this point, Yang Yuehua interjected, "On July 19th, I went to the District Office with Bao Gang. The District Chief was not at home at that time. The tea server received us. After a while, the District Chief came back. Bao Gang introduced us and asked me to call him Mr. Zhang. Later, I stayed at his

second wife's place

for more than a month. I took a photo with his second wife. I was dressed as a man in the photo. The photo is in the clip." Zhang Qinghong immediately refuted, "Absolutely not. I only have one wife, surnamed Yao." He said that Chuansha County has a Baojia system, and an investigation can easily clarify the matter. The presiding judge said, "There is no need to argue. This is easy to investigate. However, you are the District Chief. Did this happen or not? If you deceive me, you are deceiving the Supervisory Yuan. Deceiving the Yuan is deceiving our party, and deceiving the party is being a reactionary." Zhang replied, "Since my student days, I have dedicated myself to the party. I am wholeheartedly working for the party. I would never deceive the party. Please investigate thoroughly." At this point, Yang Yuehua again

attacked

Zhang Qinghong, saying that he graduated from Chi-chih University in Jiangwan and was a classmate of Bao Gang. But Zhang denied it. At this point, Bao Gang still denied the matter with Yang Yuehua, insisting that he was being framed. The judge then said, "I also hope that this didn't happen. If this happened, it would be very painful. Lawyers are supposed to protect human rights. Now, if a lawyer has done this, it would be a laughingstock both domestically and internationally. It would be unthinkable." Then he asked Bao's tea server, Zhang Xingu, who replied, "I have been a tea server for ten months, and I have also been framed." At this point, the supervisory committee member said, "Bao Gang's case is being judged by the court. What I am reviewing is the public official, District Chief Zhang Qinghong, and Zhang Datong and others. So now I will take this

copy of the record

back to discuss what crime Zhang Qinghong has committed and what crime Zhang Datong has committed." At this point, Cui Changgui made a written statement, "If Yang Yuehua is not found at the District Chief's house, I am willing to accept whatever punishment." At this point, the judge ordered Zhang Qinghong to also make a statement that if Bao Gang and Yang Yuehua were hiding in his house, he was also willing to be punished. At this point, the supervisory committee member had finished questioning everyone. He then asked Judge Xie to return to court to continue questioning the original case of hindering family happiness. Judge Xie then took out Zhang Qinghong's four-inch

photo

and asked, "Is this your photo?" He replied, "Yes." He asked, "Why did it fall into Yang Yuehua's hands?" He replied, "I don't know." The judge then showed a double photo, instructing the photo with a man dressed as Yang Yuehua, and a woman dressed up. The judge then asked, according to Yang Yuehua, the woman is your concubine, he replied, "I do not have a concubine, I only have one wife, Yao, who is 31 years old and can be brought in." At this point, the judge announced that the case would be adjourned for further questioning. The defendant Bao Gang was fined an additional 1,000 yuan bail, which was posted by Wang Zechang from Wang Shunxing Wood Shop at 743 Min'guo Road, Laobeimen. Zhang Xingu was taken into custody without bail. Court adjourned after 7 p.m.

China Health Society Established Yesterday, Popularizing Public Medical Security, Promoting Preventive Healthcare

The China Health Society, which has been in preparation for years, is the latest medical service organization of the Municipal United People's Physicians Hospital. Years ago, Dr. Ding Huikang, the director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium, was ordered by the Ministry to go abroad to study and had a cooperative agreement with the Navo Company of Hamburg, Germany, the largest social insurance organization in Germany. After returning to China, he actively advocated for in-depth discussions with domestic experts and received support from former Mayor Zhang Dingfan and other parties. Preparations were completed, and the society was officially established yesterday, commencing services. The details are recorded as follows:

Benefiting the Poor

The society is specifically for the general poor people. Due to the decline of the social economy, it is difficult for the general public to afford medical treatment. This situation has worsened in recent years, which affects not only personal happiness and hinders social construction, but also seriously damages the foundation of national health and revival. In view of this, the society aims to enable anyone to solve all medical problems with a small number of limited community fees and obtain the most effective health protection. Li Chao stated that the society's work is the foundation of national defense.

Centralized Medical Care

Our country has never had a health organization that brings together the public's doctors and hospitals. The Society is adapting to the needs of society, centralizing all of the latest medical equipment from the modern world, establishing a large-scale medical service organization, popularizing public medical security, and promoting preventive healthcare.

Contracted Doctors

The Society has contracted specialist doctors from all departments to serve members on a regular basis. The specialists in each department are Dr. Ding Huikang, Director of Cardiology; Dr. Wang Yihui, Director of Gynecology and Obstetrics; Dr. Gu Honglie, Director of Radiology; Dr. Yi Hou, Director of Pediatrics; Dr. Jiang Junsun, Director of Infectious Diseases; Dr. Li Zubai, Director of Gastroenterology; Dr. Sun Kejin, Director of Dermatology; Dr. Dong Bingqi, Director of Surgery, Thoracic Surgery, Reproductive Urology; Dr. Lin Shixi, Director of Ophthalmology, Otolaryngology; Dr. Qu Songshou, Director of Laboratory; Dr. Tang Jingheng, Resident Director. In addition, famous doctors from various departments are specially contracted for joint collaboration. In addition to the Hongqiao Sanatorium and its branches, which initiated the Society and provide all medical equipment, the entire city's hospitals are specifically used for joint collaboration to meet the needs of patients.

Free Rights

The Society divides members into three types, A, B, C, and D, as well as affiliated members, according to the social and economic situation, so that each can pay community fees economically according to their personal circumstances. Once a member joins the society, they are entitled to various medical benefits in accordance with the regulations. On average, a daily fee of 1.6 cents entitles them to free consultations throughout the year. A daily community fee of 3 cents entitles them to free hospitalization and all medical expenses. Therefore, once a member joins the society, the problem of medical treatment is completely resolved.

Preventive Work

Modern medicine is advancing rapidly. In the passive aspect, emphasis is placed on treatment, while in the active aspect, attention is paid to preventing diseases. The society plans to implement examinations for tuberculosis, cancer, venereal diseases, trachoma, and free health checkups to promote preventive medicine and enable the public to achieve true health protection. Staff members will visit members' daily lives and hygiene methods at any time and provide detailed guidance to improve family health and happiness.

Suburban Entertainment

In order to improve the health of members and adjust their lives, the Society has selected scenic suburban areas with convenient transportation and established suburban clubs. It also provides buses and all legitimate entertainment facilities such as tennis courts and boating, and can also provide social accommodation at the lowest price, improving health in entertainment.

Ten-Year Plan

The health care business is still in its infancy in our country. The Society has a ten-year plan. In the first year, the society will make the public aware of the truth of health care and service conditions as a period of awareness. In the second and third years, the society will do its best to serve with the public's awareness and a solid foundation as a service period. After the third year, it will strive for development so that national health care can achieve great results as a promotion period. From the fifth to the tenth year, it hopes that all localities will respond and set up more branch offices as a period of popularity, which is also the period of success for China's health care business.

Supervisory Titles

The Society has received enthusiastic support from leaders from all walks of life. The supervisors are Li Dachao, Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Yan Fuqing, and Lu Bohong. The directors are Ye Gongchuo, Zhang Dingfan, Zhou Yongneng, Feng Bingnan, Zhu Shaoping, Jiang Wenyu, Weng Zhilong, Zhu Boquan, Cai Chengxin, Du Chongyuan, Wang Boqi, Ma Yinliang, Zheng Yaonan, Ding Fubao, and Ding Huikang.

Head Office

The Society has set up its head office at No. A2, South West Road, Jing'an Temple, Shanghai. The transportation is very convenient. Detailed articles can be obtained by sending a request to the address.

The Municipal National Products Movement Federation issued an announcement yesterday to promote family visitation work, stating that the Federation is now sincerely offering some advice to your wife and ladies of your household, because we see that the national crisis is extremely serious, on the one hand due to enemy oppression, and on the other hand due to the annual outflow of money. Municipal Federation Urges City Government to Ban Disguised Escort Services Publicly Soliciting Business with Obscene Language, Leading Weak-Willed Youths Astray

The Citizens' Federation of the First Special District of Shanghai has submitted a petition to the Municipal Government to ban disguised escort services. The original petition states: "Regarding the matter of petitioning for the banning of disguised escort services. The establishment of escort services in cities is not inherently wrong. Merchants from afar, unfamiliar with the local area, often lack knowledge of market conditions or tourist attractions. Having an escort service to guide them is convenient. Therefore, most major cities worldwide have escort services to serve the needs of merchants and travelers. The existence of escort services in Shanghai is a relatively recent phenomenon. However, due to their unscrupulous pursuit of profit, they have sprung up like bamboo shoots after rain. It is estimated that no less than a hundred have been established one after another. Upon examination, they not only lack any value in serving society but also employ absurd measures that harm society. Recently, they have even published advertisements openly soliciting business with obscene language, leading many weak-willed youths astray, unable to extricate themselves. We believe that the youth are the pillars of the nation. At this time of national crisis, it is precisely when the youth should strive to repay the country. However, these disguised escort services use young women as bait, enticing in every possible way, destroying the minds and bodies of the youth, eroding their ambition, and misleading them more than anything else. The nation and the people are suffering from adverse effects. Therefore, after deliberation by the 12th Executive Committee of this Federation, we petition the government to ban disguised escort services in order to purify public morals and safeguard the foundation of the nation. Furthermore, for escort services with pure purposes, we also request that regulations be promulgated and registration be conducted. The qualifications of the guides should be strictly scrutinized to impose limitations, so that unscrupulous elements cannot take advantage. We hereby respectfully submit this petition for review and implementation. We pray for your consideration."
