China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Announces Overview of Reorganization Efforts Salary Reduction of 10,400 Yuan After Layoffs Freight and Passenger Revenue Increases by Over 718,000 Yuan

Following the Ministry of Transportation's order for reorganization, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, under the leadership of General Manager Cai Zengji, Deputy General Managers Tan Boying and Lao Mian, has been resolutely working on reforms. Although the time has been short, significant progress has been made in organization, personnel, shipping, etc. The company has now released an overview of the reorganization efforts, which is reproduced below:

Internal Structure

Before the reorganization, the internal organization of the company, in addition to the General Manager's Office, included the Supervisory Committee and the Board of Directors. All important administrative matters had to be decided by the two committees before being implemented by the General Manager's Office. In February of this year, following the reorganization order, the Supervisory Committee and the Board of Directors were abolished. In addition to retaining the General Manager's Office, two Deputy General Managers were added. The organization names and responsibilities of the internal departments, sections, and warehouses have been slightly modified. After the reorganization, the procedures for each department, section, and warehouse to handle matters were re-established based on actual circumstances, with appropriate additions and mergers. To improve efficiency, the procedures for each department, section, and warehouse were designed to have mutual connections and checks. In particular, the regulations between the warehouse and the accounting office were made especially detailed. All receipts and payments must be mutually verified against the accounting office's books. These detailed rules have been drafted and submitted to the Ministry for review.

Layoffs and Salary Reductions

During the five years from 1928 to 1932, the average number of internal employees of the company was over 194. The highest number was 279 in the spring of 1932, with monthly salaries totaling over 33,700 yuan. By the winter of 1932, the number of employees had been reduced to 234, with salaries totaling over 26,880 yuan, already a decrease from before. After the reorganization this year, as a result of efforts to streamline operations, the number of employees has been reduced to 125, with salaries totaling over 16,480 yuan, a reduction of 109 employees and a monthly salary reduction of 10,400 yuan compared to before the reorganization.

Passenger Revenue Increase

Before the reorganization, all river steamers of the company adopted a contracted quota system. The business of each vessel was managed entirely by the business director (i.e., the comprador). There were no restrictions on the sale of passenger tickets, and undisciplined soldiers and riffraff mixed among the passengers, smoking, gambling, and creating chaos. With such disorder, hygiene was out of the question. Therefore, the treatment of passengers in the steerage was almost inhuman. In particular, the number of tea servers on each ship was often around a hundred. They received no wages and had to pay a large deposit. They would then demand tips for berths and extort wine money. The petty expenses often exceeded the ticket price by one or two times. Openly soliciting, travelers regarded river steamers with fear, and business declined as a result. After the reorganization, the comprador system was resolutely abolished on April 1. Tickets are now sold at counters at the dock and passengers board the ship with tickets, which are allocated to designated cabins. This prevents riffraff from mixing in. The tea servers were renamed "service attendants" and their wages and wine money were fixed. All bad habits were eliminated. The New Life Movement Promotion Association dispatched members to the ships to guide hygiene and other matters. The company also formed another inspection team to conduct inspections on the ships. Since implementation, travelers have found it convenient and passenger revenue has increased significantly. From the abolition of the comprador system and the adoption of the "actual reporting and actual reimbursement" system in April of this year to the end of July, after deducting business expenses, there was a surplus of over 155,525 yuan, an increase of more than 21,025 yuan compared to the contracted quota during the same period in 1935, accounting for 15.66% of the contracted quota.

Ship Repair

Ship repair costs have been extremely high annually. Before the reorganization, the repair of each ship took 60 to 70 days, or at least a month. After the repairs were completed, the ship's crew would inspect and accept the work themselves. This not only led to incomplete and dishonest work on the project, but also caused a long period of suspension, resulting in significant losses in business. Therefore, after the reorganization, when a ship needs to be repaired, the company's engineers inspect and survey the ship and submit a report to the company for approval before soliciting bids for the repairs. Engineers are then assigned to the ship to supervise the repairs and submit a supervisory report. The repairs for each ship now take only eight or nine days, or a maximum of 13 or 14 days. In total, the repair costs for all ships under the company from February to August of this year were only over 231,750 yuan, a decrease of 108,378 yuan compared to the amount spent from February to August of 1935.

Material Consumption

Without restrictions, waste is inevitable. Therefore, after the reorganization, the quantity of materials required for each ship each month was specified based on the size of the ship and reserved in advance. Public bids are solicited every three months. To the extent possible, domestic goods are used as the standard. For items needed temporarily, if the estimated value is more than 100 yuan, bids must also be solicited before purchasing. The consumption of each ship is also secretly inspected at any time to ensure that funds are not wasted and materials are not wasted. In total, the materials used by each ship from February to August of this year amounted to 87,120 yuan, a decrease of more than 66,523 yuan compared to the amount for the same seven-month period in 1935 before the reorganization.

Ship Fuel

Fuel is a major expense for the company. The long-standing malpractices in the past cannot be denied. There have been reforms in previous years. After the reorganization, the procedures for requisitioning coal were strictly regulated, and the use of coal was secretly inspected on the ships. From February to June of this year, the ships traveled 350,792 nautical miles, using 42,069 tons of coal, an average of 0.1192 tons of coal per nautical mile. Compared to the amount of coal used per nautical mile before the reorganization (0.1312 tons), there was a reduction of 0.0120 tons of coal per mile. If the average amount of coal used per mile before the reorganization is multiplied by the total nautical miles traveled in the five months of this year, then 3,955 tons of coal should have been saved, which, at a price of 11 yuan and 15 cents per ton, amounts to a total savings of over 43,998 yuan.

Labor Bidding

The company's Shanghai docks are divided into five wharves: South, North, Central, New, and Hua. The annual expenses for cargo handling labor amount to over 300,000 yuan. In the past, a contracted system was adopted, resulting in significant losses each year. After the reorganization, the Ministry of Transportation ordered the abolition of the old system and the adoption of public bidding. Public bidding was held on several occasions, with the Director of the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau sent by the Ministry to supervise the process. A Bid Review Meeting was also formed to review the bidders' experience and the prices they bid to determine the winners. The bidder with the lowest bid and the most experience was selected as the winner and the runner-up for each wharf. The process has now been completed. Although the prices bid for each wharf are not the same, the average is 67.1%. Based on the actual labor expenses for 1935, over 114,700 yuan can be saved each year. If business develops in the future and cargo volume increases, the savings will be even greater.

Business Comparison

The company's river and sea steamer revenue is mainly from passenger and freight fares. In the past, due to various reasons, business was declining. After the reorganization, efforts were made to rectify the situation, and business gradually began to thrive. From February to July of this year, both passenger and freight transportation increased, with an average increase of about 17% compared to the same period last year. In particular, passenger and freight transportation increased sharply in August. The total revenue for the month was 755,451 yuan and 2 cents, while the revenue for the same month last year was 509,868 yuan and 6 cents, an increase of 245,582 yuan and 96 cents, an increase rate of 48%. In total, the freight and passenger revenue for the seven months from January to August of this year amounted to over 4,271,170 yuan, an increase of over 718,546 yuan compared to the freight and passenger revenue for the same period in 1935.

Tensions High Between Two Factions Fruit Workers Engage in Armed Fight Workers Express Dissatisfaction with Foremen's Oppression Long-Standing Feud Between New and Old Factions Erupts Recently

The area around Beisuzhou Road and Touba Road is a gathering place for various fruit businesses. After the fruit boats from the inland areas dock at the piers there, the unloading of the fruit has been handled by workers who specialize in this trade. In recent years, these workers have mostly felt that their foreman, Li Shibaobao, a Cantonese, often oppresses the workers and deprives them of their wages, so they are very dissatisfied. They have discussed uniting to cope with the situation. Therefore, on June 15th of this year, the Shanghai Fourth District Civilian Boat Shoulder-Carrying Industry Workers' Union was organized. The first step was to gather willpower, and then to seek liberation. Li also knew the workers'

intentions

So he decided to start gradually eliminating those who disagreed with him. Therefore, he recruited 70 new workers from his hometown to join the work and used this to increase his strength. From then on, the workers in this industry formed new and old factions, which became increasingly hostile. The old faction planned that once Li was overthrown, they would support Xu Jintang, a standing committee member of the union, to become the leader. Therefore, the secret struggles between the two sides were very fierce. Until recently, the simmering tension was about to

erupt

Unexpectedly, at 1:30 PM the day before yesterday, the new and old workers had a clash at the Beisuzhou Road Pier. Each side had dozens of people. At first, they attacked each other with fists and feet, but it was not very intense. Soon, Zhang Asan from the new faction was defeated and fell into the river. Fortunately, he was rescued by a water patrol and did not drown. Then, the two sides each took up weapons. The old faction was armed with carrying poles and sticks. Because many of the new faction members were members of the Wu Song Road Guangdong Triad Society, they had

martial arts training

So they took out spears, swords, and other weapons from the society and faced off again on the riverbank. In an instant, the atmosphere there was tense, and passersby looked on in alarm. Nearby police officers, seeing this situation, quickly reported it to the

police station

Which immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to suppress the fight. The men had already stopped fighting and scattered like birds and beasts. When the detectives arrived, only Zhang Asan's brother, Azu, was left on the ground groaning. His left leg bone had been broken, and

his buttocks and back were all injured

The police arrested six old faction workers: Fang Achun, Dong Qibing, Chen Xingzhang, Wan Yulang, Zhang Chenyao, and Zhang Ailai, and five new faction workers: Xu Yonghong, Chen Wu, Chen Xiang, Chen Zhou, and Zhang Lian. They seized six carrying poles and sticks, four spears, and another weapon, and took them all back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special District Court, where Judge Dai Rongduo interrogated them. The police lawyer, Jiang Baolian, briefly described the

armed fight incident

Stating that he was prosecuting them for disturbing public order under Article 150 of the Criminal Code. As for the injured Zhang Azu, he had been taken to Tongren Hospital by the police. His injuries were not light, and the case still needed to be investigated. He requested a postponement. The defendant's old faction workers retained lawyer Li Zhongwen for their defense, while the new faction retained lawyer Wu Linkun for their defense. Because the positions of the two sides were different, their defenses contained much mutual attacks. Each side insisted on its own version of events. The court, because the facts of the case still needed to be investigated, questioned each defendant and ordered them all to be remanded in custody for further questioning next Tuesday.

Mao Yiwen, Chinese Detective Chief of the Xinzha Police Station, and detectives Wu Changkai, Xu Zhixiang, Wang Qishan, and Weng Peiyu, etc., learned that someone was organizing a cricket gambling den on the upper floor of Dou Pai Su Xi, a pig-slaughtering shop at No. 50, Lane 1050, Chengdu Road. Lost 20 Yuan Playing Jai Alai

As the boat reached the middle of the river, he suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide while the ferrymen were not paying attention. Fortunately, Chinese Police Officer No. 91 from the Customs Water Patrol Police Station arrived and helped the boatmen rescue him and bring him back to the police station. He confessed that he worked at the college and received a salary of 30 yuan per month. Unexpectedly, he recently lost 20 yuan at the jai alai stadium, which made it difficult for him to make ends meet. So, he became disillusioned with life. His family is all in his hometown. He has a cousin in Shanghai, Xia Anxiu, who is also the Dean of Studies at the college and lives at No. 23, Pushicun, Pushi Road, French Concession. The police chief believed that his confession was probably not so simple, but he did not question him further. That night, he sent Detective Gu Wenkui to his cousin's home to notify him. His male servant, Ye Chunshan, brought dry clothes to the police station to pick up Xia and take him home to comfort him.

Li Jialong to Succeed as General Manager of Sze Ming Bank

Li to Assume Office Tomorrow

Sze Ming Bank has had a solid reputation for more than 20 years since its opening. After deliberation by the joint meeting of the board of directors and supervisors of the bank, it was decided to hire Mr. Li Jialong to succeed as General Manager. It is said that Mr. Li is scheduled to assume office at the bank on the 29th of this month. Mr. Li Jialong, also known as Runsheng, is the current Manager of the Nanjing Branch of the Central Bank and is knowledgeable and experienced in finance. His appointment as General Manager of Sze Ming Bank is deeply celebrated as a great acquisition for the bank.

Russian Family's Ama Dies Tragically from Abortion

Li Zhengshi, also known as Zheng Xiuying, a woman from Hefei, Anhui, is 33 years old this year. Her husband farms in the countryside for a living. She came to Shanghai with her second son, Erbao (12 years old this year), to work as a servant. She is currently an ama for a Russian family in Room 15, Apartment 15, No. 15, Henry Road, French Concession. The mother and son live in the company's room in the employer's house. Ms. Zheng recently had an affair, resulting in pregnancy. Fearing that she would be ashamed to face her husband when she gave birth, she decided to have an abortion. On the night of the 13th of this month, between 8:00 and 9:00 PM, she hired an old midwife surnamed Wang to come to her room to administer medicine to induce an abortion. As a result, she became ill. By the 23rd, her illness had worsened. She ordered her son Bao to call her younger brother, Zheng Tingsheng (31 years old, residing at No. 183, Malang Road, working as a Sixth Two Six police officer in Dongming Deli), to come. She was sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. After the doctor's diagnosis, he reported it to the French Police Station as usual. Detectives were dispatched to question her. According to Ms. Zheng, she hired a midwife surnamed Wang, who lived at No. 6, Qiajiatang Road, Qingli, to perform the abortion. The detectives went to Qiajiatang to investigate, but there was only Dao Shengli there, not Dao Qingli. Furthermore, there was no old midwife named Wang living at No. 6, Dao Shengli, so it was impossible to investigate and arrest the person who performed the abortion. Because of her serious illness, treatment was ineffective, and she died in the hospital at around 7:00 AM yesterday. The hospital notified the police station, which sent a hearse to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch to examine the body and reported the matter to the Second Special District Court. Prosecutor Wang Ren and forensic medical officers went to the office and determined that Li Zhengshi had indeed died from illness after an abortion. Her brother claimed the body.

Woman Files Criminal Complaint After Divorce Accuses Former Husband and Lawyers

Claims She Did Not Request Divorce

After Investigation, Claim Deemed Untrue

Xu Maoqing, a 24-year-old woman from Danyang, married Zhu Changgeng, a fellow townsman who runs a small noodle shop in Shanghai, several years ago. Recently, because she wanted to divorce her husband, she hired lawyer Zhou Zhengli to file a lawsuit against Zhu with the First Special District Court for divorce and to request 4,000 yuan in alimony. Zhu hired lawyer Ye Xiazhao to defend him. During the court hearing, under the persuasion of the judge, a settlement was reached for divorce. Zhu paid the woman 500 yuan, and both parties signed the settlement record, closing the case. Unexpectedly, Xu Maoqing has now filed a criminal self-prosecution against lawyers Zhou and Ye and her former husband Zhu Changgeng, claiming that she only requested separation from Zhu at the time and did not advocate for divorce. She was actually deceived by Zhou, Ye, etc., who colluded. She also listed various crimes under Articles 120, 121, 122, 238, and 342 of the Criminal Code in the complaint, requesting that each defendant be punished according to the above articles. A few days ago, Judge Chuan Lin of the First Special Court opened a hearing. The woman failed to appear, and the hearing was postponed to yesterday afternoon. Both parties were present. However, Ye Xiazhao claimed that the woman was making false accusations, so he filed a counterclaim, requesting that she be punished for making false accusations. After Judge Chuan first questioned Xu Maoqing about the divorce settlement in court that day, because the settlement in the case was agreed to by both parties and a record had been made by the judge and court clerk, it was impossible for the lawyers of the two parties to influence it. He questioned the woman about what evidence she had to support the claim that the lawyers had accepted bribes, but Xu Maoqing could not answer. Then, Zhou Zhengli testified that the woman had expressed regret after the divorce settlement. Therefore, she must have been misled by others into thinking that the 500 yuan she received was too little, which led to her current actions of accusing the lawyers. Ye Xiazhao said that this kind of litigation on false pretenses has a real impact on the reputation of lawyers, and requested that the woman be punished according to the law. After careful investigation and inquiry, Judge Chuan found Xu Maoqing's claims to be untrue and the articles of law cited to be erroneous. Considering that the woman was ignorant, he immediately announced the verdict in court: the original lawsuit and the counterclaim were both dismissed, and neither party was guilty.

Seducing a Fiancée: Lawsuit Resolved in Court with Conditions Negotiated by the Judge

Zhang Fenglai, a Suzhou native running a mutton shop at No. 3 Xiangxin Lane, Aierjin Road, Public Concession, has a youngest daughter named Yu Zhen, also known as Xiao Meimei, seventeen years old this year. In the winter of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933], she was betrothed through a matchmaker to Shi Xiaodi (apprentice in dental inlay, sixteen years old this year and not yet a full-fledged master), the eldest son of Shi Jinsheng, a fellow townsman in the same trade residing at Peifuli, Huanghe Road, French Concession, to be his wife. After the engagement, the young couple frequently visited each other's homes. In the autumn of last year, Shi Xiaodi lured Zhang Yuzhen to his home in the Suzhou countryside and had illicit sexual relations with her, resulting in pregnancy. In the spring of this year, she gave birth to a daughter. Subsequently, animosity arose between the two families. The Shi family first filed a criminal complaint with the Special No. 1 Court, accusing Zhang Fenglai, Zhang Buqing, and Zhang Yuzhen (father, son, and daughter) of offenses such as disrupting the family, defrauding them of betrothal gifts, theft, and assault. Later, Zhang Fenglai, acting as the legal guardian, along with his daughter Yuzhen, filed a criminal self-accusation with the Special No. 2 Court, accusing Shi Jinsheng and his son Shi Xiaodi of offenses against public morals and the family. This was reported in previous issues. Now, the lawsuit in the Special No. 1 Court has been concluded. The lawsuit in the Special No. 2 Court, after repeated hearings and mediation by Judge Zhang Chao, given that both parties were in-laws and for the sake of the future happiness of their children, should not go to extremes, and were advised to negotiate a settlement out of court. The case was adjourned for further hearing. Yesterday, another summons was issued for a court hearing. The two parties still failed to reach a settlement outside of court. The court advised both parties to reach a settlement in court, setting the following conditions: 1. Before the end of the solar calendar year, Shi Jinsheng would choose a date for his son and daughter-in-law to marry; 2. Separate rooms would be provided; 3. They would cook separately; 4. Shi Jinsheng would provide rent, firewood, and rice; 5. A monthly allowance of thirty yuan for vegetables and pocket money would be provided for a year; 6. The previous betrothal gifts sent by the Qian family would not be pursued. The agreed conditions would be implemented from the date of the marriage and last for one year. After one year, Shi Jinsheng would provide a monthly subsidy of fifteen yuan for six months. Both parties, along with their children, appeared in court and expressed satisfaction with the agreed conditions. After signing the settlement record in court, the private prosecutor requested to withdraw the private prosecution. The court ruled that while Article 227, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law could be withdrawn, Articles 240, Paragraphs 1 and 3 of the Criminal Law could not be withdrawn and must be adjudicated. After the ruling, the court ruled that the case would not be heard, and the remaining parts were outside its jurisdiction. Both parties thanked the court and left. This cash reserve is deposited in the Bank's head office and branch offices: 9,016,108.1 yuan 4 jiao 8 fen; deposited with other banks: 11,001,259.9 yuan 5 jiao 2 fen. Guarantee Reserve, converted into silver yuan: 10,566,0100 yuan. (B) Total amount of Customs Gold Unit exchange certificates issued: 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. Total amount of Customs Gold Unit exchange certificate reserves: 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed editor, your newspaper published an article on the 24th, "Jiu Fu Construction Company Sues Foreigner Ju Tong for Fraud," based solely on the plaintiff's one-sided account, which is far from the truth. This matter originated from Jiu Fu and the Japanese, Amano Hachiro, having been in contact for some time, directly entering into a contract stating that the sugar factory was still in preparation and that it was planned to use the old National Factory in the future, but it had not yet been acquired. Jiu Fu, eager to get the business, voluntarily deposited a security deposit with Amano, requesting priority for future housing repairs. Ling Qihong and Mr. Liu (rumored to be not Liu Peilin) repeatedly visited Mr. Dun Gen, asking him to vouch for Amano. If the preparation failed, the security deposit would be returned. Dun Gen informed them of all he knew about the setbacks Amano had suffered in the preparation. The two gentlemen agreed to delay the matter, but then suddenly returned to pester him, expressing extreme respect. Dun Gen, moved by emotions, (1) respected the feelings of the two gentlemen and wanted to associate with them, (2) saw that their contract had the seal of the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai, proving it was not false, (3) could not resist the sweet talk of being offered the position of Chinese manager in the future, so he reluctantly signed the guarantee. However, at that time, he stated that he guaranteed the original amount of money and would not be liable for other responsibilities. Amano also personally requested a written guarantee from him, which proves that Dun Gen never participated in the internal affairs. The plaintiff's claim that Dun Gen went to the National Factory with them to direct everything is pure fantasy. Dun Gen was not present when the payment was made and was not involved in the Finance Department's appointment. Such slander is a disgrace to the moral standards of the legal profession. Furthermore, the address mentioned, No. 1 North Daihe Road, is where Amano lived. Dun Gen only stayed there for a few weeks in the spring to urge Amano to proceed or refund the money, and then left in disappointment. He had already prepared to compensate, but Amano's foreign firm had five machines that he promised to sell to offset the debt, which caused delays and ultimately led to the breakup. In short, the plaintiff should not attribute his dealings with Amano to Dun Gen. Guarantees for compensation are a civil matter and should not be brought as a criminal lawsuit to harm fellow countrymen. I humbly request your chief editor to uphold your reputation for impartiality and to make the correction. Sincerely, Wang Dun Gen, October 25, 1936, in Songjiang.

Shen Bao National Products Special

Contributions

Further Discussion on Home Visits

— Yang An

Recently, newspapers have reported on the diligence and difficulty of the home visit work of the Shanghai National Products Promotion Federation, and the self-reports of the visitors, while lamenting the difficulty of the visit work, are quite admirable for their determination and perseverance.

We believe that home visits are not difficult, but it is difficult to make each family understand the importance of the visit work. Housewives are the masters of the family. Who has no reason, who has no emotion, who is willing to take the daily necessities from imported goods? If newspapers promote them at any time, spread them in the news, write them into comments, or use text to advocate, or use pictures to express, or make good use of advertisements, or take photographs, so that everyone knows, everyone knows that national product visits are indispensable, this is one. Secondly, radio stations should introduce them well before or after the start of the program, inform them with a camera, and tell them the fun of visiting work, so that housewives can understand them in advance, understand them in their minds, and will not be incompatible once they arrive at the door, this is the second. Furthermore, women's organizations such as the Young Women's Christian Association, the Women's Temperance Association, and the Shanghai Women's Association, etc., are enthusiastic ladies who do not hesitate to bother and introduce them widely, so that housewives in each family are enthusiastic about it, and actively participate in the women's use of national products association to serve the society by themselves, all of which are the help that all parties should have. It is to increase the work efficiency of the five female visitors. I hope that all of you will love the country from now on, and make a little contribution to the national industry.

College Students and National Products

— Li Gu Jun

Promoting the use of domestic goods is originally the responsibility of the nationals of a country, especially the knowledgeable nationals should know the importance of using domestic goods. However, the situation in our country is showing an abnormal phenomenon. College students who have received higher education have long put the four words "use domestic goods" out of the nine heavens. If you don't believe it, we only need to visit any university to know that my words are correct. Now let me report the actual living conditions of college students!

1. In terms of clothing: Generally, college students who claim to be extraordinary generally think that after entering university, it is not an honor to wear a suit and leather shoes, and it is not enough to show their identity; talking about general female students, almost all of them are drawing eyebrows and eyes, perming their hair, and wearing high heels. What kind of Qiaoqi gauze and French crepe... can be used as the material for cheongsam, otherwise they will lose the rules of modern and are not enough to show their beauty.

2. In terms of diet: The school obviously has a large kitchen and a cooperative, but the price is too cheap, the side dishes are not to their taste, and there are rules for a few people to be at a table. Who wants to follow the rules when eating? A group of sharp-eyed restaurant owners, in order to cater to the psychology of college students, stipulated a kind of meal ticket system, one yuan can buy five or six, and one yuan for a big dish ticket can buy three. Each person can share the food, and the taste is of course to their liking. What's more wonderful is that the classification of restaurants is also based on the hometown of college students? What are Guangdong cafeterias, Sichuan restaurants, and Saint Anna Western Restaurants... beautiful and moving signs.

3. In terms of housing: A group of small real estate developers, in order to cater to the psychology of college students, knowing that college students do not want to live on campus, feeling all kinds of inconveniences, successively built new-style bungalows and apartment-like dormitories near the university, with all kinds of sanitary facilities. Generally, college students who are used to enjoying themselves, who would not want to stay here.

4. In terms of travel: It's no longer a problem! There are school buses in the school. If you think it is inconvenient, you only need to make a phone call, and in less than five minutes, the automobile line will send a car. Even streetcars and buses must be first-class.

After reading the above situation, the life of college students is so enviable! No, it is completely Westernized. Do they still care about the country's expectations of them in their daily lives? They have forgotten the instructions of their fathers and brothers when they left, let alone promote "using domestic goods."

According to the statistics of the Ministry of Education in the Republic of China in 19th year, there is only one college student in every 10,000 people in China. If the population of our country is 450 million, the people who have received higher education—college students—are only 45,000. Alas! If every college student wears a suit on average, and each suit is priced at 30 yuan (Note: Of course, not every college student wears a suit, and female students are an exception, but our calculation assumes that everyone has a set of suits, including female students' clothes, rouge, and the unnecessary expenses of male and female college students, etc.), it has already leaked 1,350,000 yuan a year! This is such an amazing thing!

To prevent college students from wasting, we can only beg the authorities of the university and the general parents to set an example, and ban college students from illegally consuming clothes, food, housing, etc. Only in this way can we get on the right track of "using domestic goods."

Introducing the China National Products Promotion Institute

— Tian Ran

Recently, there seems to be no good news in the national product industry, and the rampant smuggling is even more worrying. But we must know that there are still many people who are working hard on national products. We should "only ask about cultivation, not about harvest." For example, the China National Products Promotion Institute in Suzhou is a powerful group in the inland, so we should be optimistic about the future of national products.

The person in charge of the National Products Promotion Institute is Mr. Wei Shida, a Bachelor of Engineering from Jiaotong University. And he hired many vocationally trained personnel to assist him. Mr. Wei was formerly the Director of the Construction Bureau of Wuxian and Donghai Counties, a person with a scientific mind who is extremely enthusiastic about the national product business. He abandoned his official career to do this thankless social cause, which shows his ambition.

On the one hand, their work is to plan the promotion and management of products for national product manufacturers, and on the other hand, they pay more attention to market surveys and the collection of user opinions. These are not available to other national product groups. The rest of the research on products and the acceptance of agency commissions are their due tasks. In short, they do everything with scientific management, seek truth from facts, do not emphasize exaggeration, and do not aim at profits.

Their vision has many unique points. They set up the site in Suzhou, preparing to first do a unit experiment area from the six counties near Suzhou, and then gradually expand to various inland areas in the future. The reason why they are not established in Shanghai is because Shanghai can only be close to the product manufacturers, and at the same time, publicity is convenient. For promotion, we should seek to connect with consumers. This is enough to show the thorough thinking and long-term vision of the holder.

The introduction is briefly exhausted here. Finally, I hope that they will slowly expand the region, and I hope that they will contribute the precise survey results to the export manufacturers, and be able to set up factories on the spot in the future, so that the national light industry will not be completely concentrated in Shanghai, otherwise there will be unlimited crises in the future.

Note: The address of the China National Products Promotion Institute is inside Panmen, Suzhou.

Introducing Domestic Beer Bottles

— Yushu

Domestic beer, since the advent of Yantai and Five Stars, etc., has a large sales volume every year due to its excellent quality, giving imported goods a serious blow.

However, domestic beer feels that the only shortcoming is that the beer bottles are all foreign goods, because the procedure of beer manufacturing, after the beer is put into the bottle, must undergo several evaporations with very high heat, and ordinary bottles cannot withstand the heat, so they will burst, so foreign goods must be used.

Because of the problem of these beer bottles, domestic beer is often easily suspected by those who are enthusiastic about using domestic goods, so some manufacturers specially attach a statement on the beer bottles to dispel misunderstandings, but Tao is ultimately a troublesome task.

Recently, it is said that Jinghua Glass Factory has this beer bottle produced. On the one hand, this can reduce many leaks, and at the same time, it can also increase the value of domestic beer.

I hope that domestic beer will use domestic beer bottles from the next year!

Chunqiu

Glimpses

— (Tai Xuan)

A chicken lays an egg, and the egg hatches into a chick – everyone knows this. But if we want to delve further, did the chicken come first, or the egg? This question is not easy to answer. Because without the chicken, there would be no eggs, and without eggs, where would the chicken come from? Some say that poultry are all oviparous, which is true, but it is precisely because they are oviparous that this becomes a difficult and perplexing problem.

"Born in sorrow, die in comfort." Who doesn't want to live a life of ease and comfort? Who doesn't struggle to make a living from the two necessities of clothing and food? Because everyone struggles to make a living, the output of life is being expanded as much as possible every day, and thus competition arises. People are divided into the wise and foolish, the strong and weak. The result of competition is naturally the survival of the fittest. The same is true between people as between countries. When the people of one country feel that the development of their own country's livelihood cannot meet the demand, their target shifts to the neighboring country. This is called "aggression." We are now being trapped in this environment, so we are all in a state of distress, and in order to seek our livelihood, we have to constantly strive and struggle!

Women's Liberation Under X-rays

— Shuang Mi

Here, we can clearly understand the shocking achievements of modern women in the so-called "liberation" they have achieved in their struggles and efforts. In fact, although this cry has been echoing for many years, it is still a superficial "decoration". Rather than "liberation," it would be more refreshing to call it a "modern puppet."

Now, let's dissect the so-called "liberation" as follows:

Hair – Because it is "cut," you rarely see thick, long braids!

Ears – Liberated from the troublesome procedure of wearing earrings.

Eyes – Able to use a kind of "charming" attraction, and can look at people directly!

Eyebrows – Changed to be thin and long, this is to protect the beauty of the eyes!

Cheeks – After the surgery of the beauty salon, they rarely apply two points of thick lead powder containing a large amount of lime!

Mouth – Able to argue fluently in front of men!

Teeth – At least learn the small skill of chewing Luran fragrant gum.

Lips – Performing beautiful postures when kissing.

Chest – Not wearing a corset reveals its height.

Legs – Not wearing stockings is a kind of "contribution of flesh."

Feet – Walking like Manchurian women on "stilts."

This is just a "trend" because women's liberation must fundamentally progress with the advancement of the times!

Expulsion Order

— Xian Weisheng

When the author was young, he often heard his elders say: There is a folk method of "expelling guests" that is quite effective. For example, if a "rotten bench leg" of a friend comes to your house, and is bothering you and doesn't want to leave, the host, while being outwardly agreeable, only needs to secretly tell his family to put a broom behind the door, and that annoying friend will naturally feel the "urge to return," and bid farewell and leave. However, this matter is close to absurdity, and I thought it was not credible. Now, the "expulsion order" I am talking about is neither expressed in words nor requires carrying guns or sticks. Once the order is issued, the guest will naturally know to slip away tactfully.

In the past, in the officialdom, there was a custom that officials meeting each other absolutely avoided saying too much "idle" talk. After a few key points were made, they had to excuse themselves to leave. Especially inferiors to superiors, this point had to be paid attention to. Therefore, during the conversation between host and guest, if you heard a "serve tea," you should quickly be tactful and immediately shout "bring the sedan chair," bid farewell and leave. Because it is called "serving tea," in fact, it is urging you to "get lost" quickly.

At the end of the year, the owners of the show venues tell a few ballad singers to decide who will go on stage to tell their stories. Whoever tells the story the most "relaxed" is the one with the most "skill." The main story is told very briefly, and the one with the most "jokes" is the winner. At this time, if the speaker's skill is a bit "lacking," and the story is not very good, and they cannot win the audience's welcome, sorry, the shouts of "pour water" or "wring the towel" will follow. However, once this slogan comes out, listening friends, it is better to be tactful. The "waiting for the next show" person will understand, otherwise, it may make you "lose face"!

Little Lingzi and Raw Pear

— Man Zi

After watching the "Little Lingzi" produced by the Star Film Company, I thought it had the same taste as the raw pear I often chew these days: crisp, sweet, and tender, very light and cheerful, with a sense of pleasure on the tip of my tongue, but with a hint of sourness when you bite into the core. This refers to the story itself.

The entire performance is elastic. The progress of the story is not sticky or greasy, and it passes very smoothly, but there are some counter-reactions everywhere. This counter-reaction is mapped out with a relaxed technique, asking people to understand and appreciate it in the details. This is very similar to the characteristics of raw pears. Therefore, lychees can be eaten three hundred at a time, while raw pears need to be chewed slowly, piece by piece.

The performance and technique can be said to be completely consistent, so there are no overly exaggerated scenes, no deliberately added jokes. Whether it is an extremely small action or an extremely large meaning, it is performed very naturally and vividly. As Su Dongpo said, "Stop where you must stop, and do what you must do." The director has grasped this secret.

When the general public criticizes Chinese films, they always say that they are too much like civilized plays. The drawback of civilized plays is that they speak for the sake of speaking, often disregarding the plot. The dialogue of Little Lingzi is able to suit the plot. When it should be fast, it is never delayed, and when it should be slow, it is never slippery. Its highs and lows, strengths and weaknesses, are consistent with the melody of the performance as the plot progresses.

This film is not only unique in the Star Film Company, but also a creation in the past domestic films. Cheng Bugao has already shown his transformation technique in "New and Old Shanghai," and in Little Lingzi, it is a transformation.

These days can be called the "raw pear season," then the raw pear-like "Little Lingzi" is exactly what we need, and a feast for the eyes. Therefore, putting aside consciousness, it is also a masterpiece.

In Memory of Mr. Lu Xun

— Zhou Shoujuan

Exhausted years "outcrying," the public then succeeds, dead end, "wandering," where do I return?

"Outcry" and "Wandering" are collections of short stories written by Mr. Lu Xun, which I deeply admire.

Changing Nest Luan and Phoenix

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seven: High Fraternal Love Hides Letter Pitying Weak Sister, Strong Poetic and Scholarly Air Peeks at Shadow Laughing at Cold Scholar

He stretched out his head and smelled the Pearl Orchid, and said with a smile, "Does Cousin really like light green?" Guoqi said, "How can you tell?" Youmei said, "Because orchids are light green." Guoqi laughed, "So that's how you figured it out. Actually, I don't care that much about orchids. I love all flowers that are quiet and not too seductive." Youmei said, "Isn't it better for flowers to be more beautiful? Why don't you like those that are too beautiful?" Guoqi smiled and said, "That's because of what Ms. Li said about being rich in poetry and books." Youmei saw that although he was constantly laughing and talking, he was wearing a long gown and sitting upright, and he was not very natural. Especially the slight beads of sweat on his forehead showed that he was impatient. She stood up and said, "Auntie, let's go outside to the hall to sit." Cousin, you should do your homework. Guoqi said, "Although there is wind in the hall, it is not as cool as this room." Youmei smiled. "Cousin, I don't think you need to be polite. If I sit here, you can't take off your long gown. If you accompany us to sit outside, you have to put on your long gown. It's too impolite for a guest. I have some things I want to ask my cousin for advice. But I've decided, cousin, don't be too polite with me." Guoqi couldn't find anything to say to answer him, so he just smiled. He had no choice but not to come out to accompany the guests. Youmei arrived at the hall, and through a bamboo curtain, she kept looking inside. The white figure flickered a little at first, and then disappeared, and even the sound was gone. Youmei talked with Aunt Zhang for two hours. The sun was already setting, so she got up to say goodbye. When Aunt Zhang sent him to the patio, he turned around and walked to the door of the study, and first shouted, "Cousin, I'm leaving, see you next time." As he spoke, he lifted the hanging bamboo curtain. But he saw him lying on his desk, putting a very beautiful foreign stationery in front of him, and writing a letter with a steel pen dipped in blue ink. And the words he wrote were in English. This was a very ordinary thing for students, but it left an impression in his mind, and he felt that it was worth the trip? (91)

Crab Miscellany

— Ying Dai

Once Mid-Autumn Festival is over, crabs immediately replace mooncakes on the market, and it is another season for eating crabs. In the city of Shanghai, we can see the sale of Yangcheng Lake crabs everywhere in the crab stalls. I always feel that the crabs bought are soft and tasteless, far less delicious than the crabs produced in my hometown of Songjiang.

The reason is that the crabs produced in our hometown, although not as large as the so-called Yangcheng Lake crabs in Shanghai, are much more delicious than Yangcheng Lake crabs in terms of taste. I haven't tasted the taste of crabs from my hometown for a long time. Until last year, my family sent a basket of crabs, and I compared them with Yangcheng Lake crabs on the spot. Indeed, the crabs from our hometown are much more delicious, so my advocacy for eating crabs is not about size, but about whether the crab meat is delicious.

In autumn, the fishermen in my hometown are all energized and focused on the work of catching crabs. Some use nets, some use crab traps, and they can catch crabs worth hundreds of dollars in a crab market. It is also a huge income. However, catching crabs is always done at night, setting up lights and nets, and staying up all night, which is also very hard.

When we were young, after eating crabs, we had to keep the crab dice and put them in a charcoal basket. We walked to the river and sank the charcoal basket to the bottom of the river. In less than a quarter of an hour, we picked up the charcoal basket and often caught a few eels and small fish, which we used as a pastime.

After the crab shells are washed, dried, and ground into powder, they are burned with Atractylodes and Angelica dahurica, and all the windows and doors are closed tightly. All the bedbugs in the room can be killed within two hours. It is a good method for killing bedbugs, but people have to leave when burning.

Travels in Suzhou

(Ten years ago, I visited this state with my deceased friend. Today, returning again, the wind and rain fill the sky, I cannot bear the abdominal pain.)

The hegemonic cause of the King of Wu has long ceased to exist, the palace terraces of a thousand years fall in the setting sun, it should be that the spirit has transformed into a huge stone, gazing at the lake to await the return of the beauty. (There is a stone turtle in front of the Xizi Dressing Table, named Bird Turtle Gazing at Taihu Lake)

Yu Ran watched the osmanthus flowers in those years, on the returning boat he recalled the autumn colors in his drunkenness, still today at the place where poems are inscribed on the white wall, how many tourists speak of the Shi family. Miscellaneous Talk

The Most Economical New Women's Clothing

— Ou Si

Shanghai is China's largest money-consuming den. Generally, wealthy officials, merchants, and playboys like to transport the money they have collected in batches to Shanghai to spend, and a larger part of it is spent on women, and their money is completely consumed on clothing. Girls love nature, and they originally specialize in competing for beauty in clothing. Anyway, when they buy their favorite items, someone will willingly rush to pay the bill for them, without having to pay out of their own pockets, and they are happy to be generous with other people's money, indulging in luxury and wasting arbitrarily. Even if it is unavoidable, and they sometimes have to use their personal savings, it is okay for them to spend money like dirt, and they are not very cherishing. Wealthy daughters and courtesans are naturally overspending, but some small family women are accustomed to the luxurious appearance of wealthy women. They can't resist the temptation of materials, and they are jealous. They are unwilling to abide by their duties, and they deliberately imitate wealthy women, trying to get a little bit of silk and fragrance, fearing that they will mess up their hair and clothes, and bury their innate beauty. Gold, pearls, jade, and diamonds are worth millions, and of course the poor cannot reach them. Only clothing is one item that they can spend all their energy on, barely piecing together one or two pieces, allowing them to imitate Xizi's frown. Therefore, Shanghai's silk shops and tailors rely on women as their only major customers. In the past ten years, there has been a so-called new clothing company, which has emerged in response to the trend. For a time, they have sprung up like mushrooms, adding dozens of companies, and each one is doing booming business and is considered the easiest way to make money at present. Many artists, whose learning is not used, and whose strengths are violated, cannot make a living from art in China. Taking advantage of the opportunity, they have joined the new clothing companies one after another, becoming drawing and design pattern makers.

At the beginning of the establishment of the new clothing company, it was able to prescribe the right medicine and make ten times the profit, because "new clothes are not pressing," which has been the case since ancient times. Those modern women have already reached the peak of selecting beautiful clothing materials, and they cannot be more picky. They have to start a new stove and strive for novelty in form, and they really need someone to come up with ideas and change patterns for them. They don't care about spending a few more dollars at all. It is said that at that time, a very ordinary blue cloth cheongsam would actually sell for twelve or thirteen yuan after the new clothing company's process. It is even more common for expensive materials to cost from tens of yuan to hundreds of yuan per piece. In Shanghai, only women's money is the easiest to cheat! In the past, although women's clothes often changed patterns, they could still maintain the status quo for a year or two. Recently, however, it has progressed like flying. Before two or five months, they have already changed completely. It has become mysterious and unpredictable. The new clothes made in the spring will be laughed at by the public as ancient monsters and outdated styles when they are worn out again in the fall. Therefore, women's clothes are not worth much after they are made. Those that cost dozens of dollars to make, even if they are still brand new and have never been worn, can only be pawned for one or two dollars in the pawnshop, which is considered good. Recently, they simply refuse to accept them because the styles change too quickly. If they are not redeemed when they expire, there is no other way except to send them to the antique display cabinet!

However, in the past year or two, the new clothing company has also become the end of its rope. This is nothing more than being affected by the recession. In today's poor and exhausted people, who has the extra strength to provide their spoiled wife and friends with six-sided renovations? This summer, due to the needs of the times, they invented a very economical new outfit. They only need to spend a few yuan to cut a few feet of black Xiangyun yarn to make a cheongsam. From famous ladies, singing and dancing stars, to the courtesans, to the sisters-in-law in the attic, they no longer have to wear other clothes. They only need to wear a pair of triangular shorts, and even the pants can be saved. With bare legs and feet, they wear a pair of leather shoes with bright red painted toes. In total, it only costs five or six yuan, and they already have everything they need from head to toe. They are like a very beautiful modern girl. What a cheap and good thing!

If we only observe from the surface, this may not be good news to raise the voice of thrift, but the cost of each clothing material is only one or two yuan, while the tailor's wages cost more than two or three yuan, which has a tendency to be top-heavy! Alas! The Shanghai women who are fond of vanity and like to waste money actually think about saving money. The degree of exhaustion of social finance can be imagined!

Page 17

The Road to Health

—Edited by Kangjian Medical Society

Yarn and Flowers: Outside Factories Continue to Sell Surplus, Cotton Yarn Price Decline Intensifies, Many Speculators Close Positions, Market Prices Increasingly Difficult to Sustain

The yarn market is trending weak, and the price decline is intensifying. Although it is usually the time for the October futures delivery to be actively sold, the factories unexpectedly delivered a total of 1,000 bales of 20-count "Yu Cheng," "Double Deer," "Golden Pagoda," and other yarns. This caused great disappointment and a blow to confidence in the market. At the same time, the prices of Japanese yarn warehouse receipts and one-week futures differed by more than ten yuan, and they were sold off aggressively in the market, further depressing market sentiment. Current yarn, due to its high price, is even more stagnant. Therefore, outside factories continue to sell surplus inventory.

Nearly 4.8 Yuan Plummet in Recent Month

The cotton yarn market opened weakly. Due to the arrival of new yarn last month and the relatively soft delivery prices, confidence was weak. In addition, due to excessive prices, all parties needed to remain stagnant, and there were few new buyers. The market trend inclined downwards, step by step. However, a certain gentleman still held a long position, but foreign merchants were bearish and sold off continuously. As a result of the bidding, each month's closing price fell by 1.3, 4, 5, and 9 jiao (tenths of a yuan) to 2.1 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. The afternoon opening saw the market trend further weaken, and spot yarn transactions halted, with many speculators closing positions. Market prices were difficult to support. Distant months were also affected and declined. The future trend depends on actual demand. As a result, the November price fell another 2.7 jiao compared to the morning closing price, and distant prices fell 7 jiao to 1.2, 5, and 6 jiao. It was found that 3,100 bales of Hengyi, 1,350 bales of Jifeng, 1,100 bales of Tonghe, 1,000 bales of Dafeng, 3,850 bales of Hexing, 2,300 bales of Senkang, 1,050 bales of Changfeng, 1,800 bales of Xincheng, 1,250 bales of Tongji, 700 bales of Minghua, and 700 bales of Zhenda were sold. Purchases included 1,950 bales of Mingde, 1,050 bales of Yukang, 2,700 bales of Yuda, 1,300 bales of Jinchang, 4,250 bales of Gengfeng, 1,100 bales of Changji, 3,650 bales of Weiyu, 1,900 bales of Dachangcheng, and 2,700 bales of Runkang. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed on the left.

Only 300 Bales of Yarn Sold

The sales of current yarn remained sluggish. It was found that all guilds bought a total of 300 bales throughout the day, and the selling price fell by 2.3 yuan. The purchase amount of each guild is as follows:

American Cotton Plummets for Seven Consecutive Days, Bidding Price Spirals Downward, Prices Fall Around One Yuan Each Month

The cotton market is declining because American cotton has plummeted for seven consecutive days, and the situation is very weak. Longs are panicking, and the trading floor is loose. The market price is falling step by step. This month, the price broke through the one-yuan mark, and the forward prices all broke through the two-yuan mark. Sales at current cotton factories have stagnated.

Nearly One Yuan Decline Recently

The bidding for cotton opened with a weak trend, because 70,000 to 80,000 dan (a unit of weight) of old, coarse cotton were delivered the previous day. Although this batch of goods was bought by fellow traders, it will not be easy to sell it all. In addition, the decline in American cotton is very intense, which has dampened market confidence. The market price is falling step by step, but most cotton merchants are consistently absorbing and anticipating a rise. As a result of the bidding, the closing prices for each month fell by 0.45 to 0.56 jiao compared to the previous day's closing price. The afternoon opening saw the current month's momentum quite weak, with few buyers in the market, and the market price became increasingly loose. Each closing price fell by 3, 4, and 6 jiao compared to the previous month's closing price. It was found that 4,400 dan of Juxing, 1,300 dan of Tongji, 1,800 dan of Kang, 1,100 dan of Jifeng, 2,700 dan of Xiaoyi, 1,600 dan of Shenchang, 1,600 dan of Ren, 2,500 dan of Yikang, 1,000 dan of Yuanxingchang, 1,200 dan of Xinchang, 3,500 dan of Minghua, and 3,200 dan of Senlian were sold. Purchases included 4,300 dan of Runlian, 4,700 dan of Chang, 4,000 dan of Tongfu, 3,400 dan of Dafeng, 2,100 dan of Jinchang, 8,400 dan of Mingde, 14,500 dan of Gengfeng, 2,800 dan of Fengtai, 1,600 dan of Changfeng, 3,000 dan of Shengyuan, 2,300 dan of Yuanda, and 1,700 dan of Shenji. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed on the left.

Sales at Current Cotton Factories have Stagnated

The consumption of current cotton is quite low, the factory's appetite is blocked, and the sources are 2,150 bales of Yao cotton and 1,820 bales of Tong cotton.

Ginning Report Favors Sellers, American Cotton Falls More Than Ten Points

Yesterday, American cotton opened with prices ranging from unchanged to falling by 3 points. Early in the morning, longs closed out positions, cotton farmers sold short, and the stock market was weak. The ginning report favored sellers, and market sentiment was sluggish. Traders continued to buy on price dips, and shorts covered their positions due to rain in the west. However, most buyers remained on the sidelines, waiting for the next government estimate. Spot cotton prices were able to maintain. The closing price fell by 12 points for spot cotton and 12 to 14 points for futures. English spot cotton fell by 4 points, and futures fell by 23 points. Indian cotton rose due to the rise in Japanese yarn, short covering, and a lack of sellers. Pingguo rose by 0.75 to 1 rupee, Aomula rose by 0.75 to 1.25 rupees, and Bai Luo Creek rose by 1 rupee. The original telegram is on the left (dated the 26th).

According to a Mumbai telegram, the opening forecast for the 27th was: Bai Luo Creek at 218 rupees, down 1.75 rupees; Aomula at 194 rupees, down 2.5 rupees; and Pingguo at 155 rupees, down 2.75 rupees.

Last Week's Cotton Exports from Rangoon

A Mumbai telegram dated the 26th stated that the amount of cotton exported from Rangoon last week totaled 268 tons, all destined for Osaka.

American Cotton's Sixth Ginning Report A Washington telegram dated the 26th stated that the Department of Commerce's Bureau of Statistics released the sixth ginning report today as follows (in thousands of bales):

Three-Product Yarn Expected to Continue Rising Two Yuan Soon

An Osaka telegram dated the 27th stated that three-product futures yarn rose by one yuan to falling by 0.3 yuan, with the near month at 221.6 yuan and the distant month at 207.4 yuan. Cotton futures fell by 0.4 to 0.5 yuan, with the near month at 64.7 yuan and the distant month at 65.35 yuan.

Piece Goods: Cotton Cloth Follows Yarn Prices Downward

Yesterday, the cloth market was affected by the current downward trend in bidding yarn and spot yarn. The cost of various cotton cloths gradually decreased, and actual sales stagnated, leading to a downward trend in cloth prices. White goods, fine cloth, fine twill, city cloth, and 84 cloth all fell (per piece) by 0.05 to 0.1 yuan. Printed flannel, serge, and line wool fell (per yard) by 0.0025 to 0.01 yuan. Jardine Matheson's Golden Pagoda bleached cloth opened for sale yesterday at 9 yuan per piece, a decrease of 0.25 yuan compared to the previous hand's selling price. Miscellaneous brand, locally produced lower-grade bleached cloth also fell (by 0.22 yuan per piece). Customers from various guilds temporarily adopted a wait-and-see attitude due to expectations of further declines, but orders continued to arrive. The Cantonese guild purchased more than 400 bales of heavy-weight 16-pound and 14-pound coarse cloth from local factories for several days. — I

Marriage issues are quite complicated. Not only does each country have its own marriage system, but each region also has its own marriage system. Some are polygamous, as in ancient China, and some are polyandrous, as in certain parts of Southeast Asia, where brothers jointly marry one wife. Marriage in our country used to be the so-called autocratic marriage, or a marriage for sale. The only condition for a marriage for sale was "matching social status." In other words, it was a matter of family status. What does "matching social status" mean? It means the rich marry the rich, the powerful marry the powerful, or the powerful marry the rich, and the rich marry the powerful. It can also be an example of matching social status. Now that freedom of marriage has become law, the old system has been completely abolished.

Recently, the great uproar in England over King Edward's love affair with Mrs. Simpson shows that the concept of social status or class in England is very deep. The British have always been known for their "gentlemanly manners," and their gentlemanly style still prevails today. Mrs. Simpson is the wife of a London stockbroker. It has recently been rumored that she is in the process of divorce and is preparing for further developments with the King in the capacity of a holiday companion. This has created a problem. It is considered a very extraordinary and terrible thing in the eyes of the British for the head of England to want to marry a commoner woman, not only a pure woman but also a married woman.

Thus, the King's love affair has become a very good topic of conversation. According to a London telegram on the 17th, King Edward was furious because the leaders of the political and religious spheres in England wanted to interfere in his friendship with his holiday companion, Mrs. Simpson. It is said that the Archbishop of Canterbury and Prime Minister Baldwin recently made an informal visit to Buckingham Palace to advise the King to be more cautious in his relationship with Mrs. Simpson. The King was extremely angry at their interference in his personal life, but he did not want to show it. He trembled his lips slightly and asked the Archbishop and the Prime Minister not to interfere in other people's affairs. The phrases "trembled his lips" and "did not want to show it" fully demonstrate that although the King had committed this scandalous love affair, he did not have the courage to actively resist the criticism from public opinion and the interference from politics and religion.

Furthermore, according to British telegrams, many people in England today imagine that King Edward VIII may abdicate his throne to his brother, the Duke of York, and retire to a happy country gentleman. The court claims that the talk of abdication is completely unfounded, but those who imagine this have various bases, etc. This kind of statement clearly indicates that to marry Mrs. Simpson, unless you sacrifice your throne and become a country gentleman, otherwise, in any case, you should sever the relationship with Mrs. Simpson. Should the king sacrifice his throne? Or should he maintain his love? The King should carefully choose one of the two. Although this meaning is not explicitly stated, the intention is already implied.

According to a London telegram on the 22nd, people close to King Edward's traveling companion, Mrs. Simpson, today declared that Mrs. Simpson really does not want to marry King Edward to avoid making things difficult for England. She also knows that the national atmosphere is not good for this matter. According to the News Chronicle, the proof copy of the previous day published a long news story that the King could marry a commoner, saying that the law allows the King to choose a commoner as his queen. However, this news was immediately deleted, which shows that even with the dignity of a monarch, one cannot marry a civilian woman. How difficult is it to remove social status!

A Visit to the Mingyuan Mushroom Farm

— Fang Zhou

(Special Report by This Newspaper) The new method of growing mushrooms is a newly discovered emerging industry in our country. Several companies in this city have already started growing them, including Sino-American, Great West, Huang's, and Mingyuan. Sino-American is said to be the earliest, and there are also many private family mushroom farms. However, because the output is still not very high, the price is very expensive, and eaters are limited to Westerners and high-end banquets.

The business of growing mushrooms has always existed in our country, but because the old traditional methods are used, they are often limited by weather and location, and ten types of mushrooms can only be dried. New-method mushrooms can not only be sold fresh, but the growers also make a good profit. Therefore, I think this is also a sideline worth promoting.

In order to learn more about the new method of growing mushrooms and the layout of the farm, I made a special trip to the Mingyuan Mushroom Farm on East Sports Association Road yesterday afternoon to conduct an on-site visit.

(1) A Glimpse of the Farm The farm is square, covering an area of more than ten acres, surrounded by fences. The single-story flat building in the front includes offices, reception rooms, and the food and dormitories for workers and staff. Behind it is a large open space, filled with piles of horse manure. Several workers are manipulating it. Next to it is a pile of mud. These new muds seem to be from other

Page 20

brought from other places. The middle building is the mushroom cultivation room. To the left is a small house where water heating is located, and a water storage pavilion is right at the entrance of the heating room.

The structure of the mushroom room is very special. There is only one door on the wall, but it is kept tightly closed all day long. Except for things going in and out, it is usually absolutely not allowed to open; every two feet on the upper end of the wall has a small circle opening, and the same small window holes are also about one foot above the ground, and can be opened and closed to adjust the temperature and climate in the room. The room is very dark, and a kind of damp smell is filled in it; I was led in by a manager with a flashlight. Because the ground was very wet, I stepped on a board and looked around. I saw water heating pipes installed all around, and two wooden racks on both sides, with four rectangular wooden trays on them. The larger one is eight square feet each. Each plate is covered with a layer of new mud, and countless snow-white things are showing through on the mud surface, and that is the newly emerging mushroom.

These mushrooms are large, some are as small as fine beads, and some can only be seen as a bit of white trace on the mud surface.

(2) Planting Method After visiting everywhere, we returned to the reception room; at this time, the manager told us about the mushroom planting method and the source of the seeds.

This mushroom seed is completely purchased from the United States, but there are many types in the United States, and the prices vary. The purchase is calculated by bag, and the size of the bag is based on the standard of seeding several square feet of area. The appearance of the seeds is like brownish-gray fine ash, which can fly if blown or brushed. As for the planting method, the horse manure is first manipulated manually in the sun. After a certain number of days, the stinky smell has been completely removed, and there is no smell at all, and all the heat has completely disappeared. Then, evenly spread it in the wooden trays. After spreading it evenly, take an equal amount of mushroom seeds and scatter them on the horse manure surface, and then spread a layer of new mud that is neither too thin nor too thick on top.—This new mud, clay and sand should not be used, only sandy loam is suitable.

After sowing, the air in the room must be closed, and no light can pass through. The average temperature is 70 degrees, and water must be poured every day. Small mushrooms can be seen in half a month, but they grow and reproduce very quickly, so after seeing small mushrooms, you can choose to cut the large ones in three or four days, cut as you go, and if you don't cut them, they will naturally wither. In this way, you can cut and produce every day for as long as four months or as little as three months, and then you must replant.

(3) Production and Promotion The production volume is large, and each square foot of area can produce up to one pound of mushrooms per day. According to the current selling price, it is worth one yuan in legal currency, but it is better to reproduce during warm weather, and it is inevitable that it will be slightly inferior in winter. However, fresh mushrooms are rarely seen on the market now, and there are not many planters, and few people eat them, so the mushrooms in the farm are sold by the farm's personnel, in addition to the daily amount agreed upon by various households.

Fresh mushrooms cannot be exposed to wind and light, otherwise they will change color, so after cutting them from the mud, put them into boxes immediately, and they cannot be stored overnight, otherwise the color will not be very white.

This fresh mushroom tastes very delicious, tender, and fatty. It is not only excellent for making dishes, but also can be made into canned food. Therefore, this mushroom business has been very developed in Europe, America, and Japan, but our country has only recently had someone advocating planting.

Mingyuan Mushroom Planting was founded last year. Although they have sown seeds twice in the past, it is said that the results are not close to the budget. As for the results of this time, because sowing has only been more than a month, it cannot be predicted, but the results are always better than the previous two times.

Finally, I asked the manager again, does China have its own mushroom seeds? Can it also be grown using improved methods? Can the improved mushrooms also collect seeds themselves in the future? He said: China also has mushroom seeds, and they can also be grown using new methods, but the results are not very good. As for collecting mushroom seeds from improved mushrooms, they still don't know how.

Depending on the Eldest Daughter-in-Law

— Shi Xi

One day, Mother told everyone that Yang Haiyun had brought a twelve-year-old girl named Jinzhi to be his daughter-in-law, to be matched with his four-year-old son, Huocong. He was a tenant farmer of our Si family, and his family only had a wife and that four-year-old son. Every season, he was busy with the fields and also busy going up the mountain to make earthen farming tools. Therefore, no one took care of his four-year-old son, and no one cooked for them. So he took such a big daughter-in-law, also for this reason.

Not long after, the time for collecting rent arrived. Fourth Aunt and the others were going to collect rent. That day happened to be my Sunday. To pick chestnuts and persimmons, I went with her to Yang Haiyun's house. It was almost eleven o'clock, and there was no one at his house, only that eleven or twelve-year-old little daughter-in-law and her four-year-old little husband.

She was thin, her face was very dark, with patches of red and black, and her voice was very small. Her eyes were often wet, and her hands were rough and large. She was wearing torn and tattered clothes, with her arms, back, and chest exposed.

She told us that Yang Haiyun had not returned yet, and then she carried her little husband to the kitchen to cook.

The next-door neighbor was also our tenant farmer. A woman heard us talking, ran over to invite us in, poured tea, and cooked some cornbread for us to eat. Fourth Aunt casually asked about Yang Haiyun's daughter-in-law, and the woman sighed repeatedly, saying:

"What a sin, old master's family! Have you seen how Haiyun's mother treats this adopted daughter-in-law (child bride)? She beats her to death or half to death. She has to cook three meals a day, fetch water herself, and go up the mountain to gather vegetables and firewood. She also has to take care of the house and watch the children. Sometimes, if she is late cooking, Haiyun's mother steps in the door, looks at the kitchen, and if the food is not ready, she starts cursing, and at the same time, the wooden stick in her hand hits her body fiercely, almost every day like this..."

Before she finished speaking, we heard footsteps outside the door. The adopted daughter-in-law came in, saying that Yang Haiyun had returned and invited us to eat. We went over and sat down for a short time, and then we heard someone crying softly. We asked and learned that Haiyun's mother had started beating the daughter-in-law again.

Although this little daughter-in-law was so short and thin, she was very good at doing things. Every day, besides cooking, taking care of the house, and looking after her little husband, she sometimes had to go up the mountain to make farming tools. When it was harvest time, Haiyun's mother always asked her to do heavy work. Sometimes she had to carry sweet potatoes from the mountain back home, about eighty or ninety pounds. As soon as she put down the sweet potatoes, she had to carry manure and ash (fertilizer mixed with urine and ash) up the mountain. If she walked too slowly, she would be hit with a hoe. Haiyun himself couldn't stand it, but he was afraid of his wife and didn't dare to say anything.

One day, the adopted daughter-in-law secretly ran to Yang Zicheng's house next door to cry and complain to Yang Ersao. Yang Ersao was a straightforward person and said casually:

"You are so young and you get beaten twice a day, you might as well die..."

She secretly remembered this in her heart. When she got home, she broke a bowl and was beaten by Haiyun's mother and didn't get any food. When it was twelve o'clock at night, she secretly got up, took the opium she had hidden under her bed, and mixed it with white wine and drank it. At five o'clock, her mother-in-law called her to get up and cook breakfast. She called several times but didn't hear her answer. She thought she was fast asleep, got up, took off the quilt, and hit her hard a few times, then went angrily to the kitchen to start a fire. After she started the fire, she still didn't see her get up, so she went to call her a second time and found out that she had died from smoking opium.

This is what we heard the second time we went to her house.

Death (Part 1)

— Liao Chu Xiu

I am still young, and my concept of "death" is very vague. I know that everyone has that day, but I always feel that "death" is very distant and vague!

I have also tried to find the concept of "death" in books, but what I got was nothing more than "gray" and "black," and "sleep"-like rest.

I think the reason why humans are afraid of death is not the pain at the time of death: because there are indeed painless ways to die in the world, and death can be used to relieve pain), but the unwillingness to be lonely. Therefore, even if someone really feels the hardship of the floating world, they are still unwilling to die decisively. "It is better to live badly than to die well," hasn't this already become a maxim?
