Drama

Wusheng Society Electricity Drama

Da Zhonghua (1160) 3:15 to 4:15 PM Music (Suzhou dialect), Song (Manna) ( )

Ah Q

Because Ah Q is a representative figure of the proletariat, he ultimately cannot but be a loyal laborer, cannot but be a lonely person with only human nature, and even cannot but be an oppressed proletarian. Also, because Ah Q is a representative figure of the uneducated class, he thinks that when doing things, it is better to be frank and tell people that he has been an accomplice in theft rather than "avoiding the issue." In love, it is better to kneel down and show her his sincere heart rather than using seductive means to win a woman's heart. In court, it is better to be a submissive lamb who is silent on the spot rather than relying on strong arguments in the hope of escaping disaster. As for the treatment and results he obtains from the environment—this is the difference between people of the propertied and propertyless classes and the educated and uneducated classes.

Ah Q, this loyal laborer, is always alive in the ears of the masses. He takes pride in eating his own strength and is proud of his sacred labor. He never values the wealthy who live in comfort and never belittles himself because of his humble occupation. He is an optimistic laborer who has no hope. However, the people in his environment all look down on him, mock him, and ridicule him. He retreats from the spirit of resistance through external challenges to the will of non-resistance through internal self-control. He retreats from "grabbing forward and hitting" to "glaring at the crowd," then retreats to "forcing self-comfort," and further retreats to admitting "I am an insect." But Ah Q is not advocating "non-resistanceism" after all. He is a worker of the uneducated class after all. In order to satisfy the expansion of his spirit of resistance, he vents his grievances on the weak and innocent little nun. Ah Q's attitude is also the attitude of the general respectable authority.

Ah Q is not only a loyal laborer, but also a single person with "humanity." He will not forget food, and he will not forget sex. Although he does not have the means and ability to seduce someone's young mistress, nor does he have a beautiful appearance to bait someone's girl, he cannot help but feel a little fluttery towards the weak and欺的小nun. He cannot help but kneel down to Wu Ma, who is "suffering from the same disease," hoping that she might be moved. But after all, he failed. Wu Ma cried and wanted to kill herself—although this was what Wu Ma meant to do to get by, Ah Q's fatal wound lies in this "must get by." Wu Ma's need to get by is caused by the environment and etiquette; Ah Q's fatal injury is caused by not knowing how to use social skills. His courtship methods are nothing more than openly "kneeling" and simply demanding "I sleep with you." Not only did his love fail, but also the labor he used to be proud of fell into the hands of Xiao X.

Fei Mu's Annual Masterpiece "Wolf Mountain Bloody Battle" Completed

Fei Mu's new work of this year after "Ethics," "Wolf Mountain Bloody Battle" (sound dialogue film), was completed a few days ago. This film was produced in collaboration with Lili Li, Zhang Yi, Han Lan'gen, Lan Ping, Shang Guanwu, Liu Qiong, Bai Lu, Hong Jingling, and Yin Xiucen, and the performance is undoubtedly perfect. The director's meticulousness and sophistication are also admired by lovers of national films. It can be called the three wonders of the second half of this year's Lianhua works with "The Lost Lamb" and "Go to Nature." The story of the film is taken from a rural area that has long suffered from wolves, writing about how to work together, unite, and exterminate the mountain wolves that harm people and animals, and finally achieve the final victory, which is very powerful and does not lose its humor. During this extraordinary period, the audience of the picture will definitely have some feelings after watching it. The film has now been submitted for inspection and will be screened simultaneously at the Xinguang Grand Theater on Ningbo Road and the Carlton Grand Theater on Parker Road in this city from the seventh of next month.

"Smuggling" Publication Announcement

The continuous comic story "Smuggling" by cartoonist Zhang Hongfei will be published on November 10. The consciousness is pure, spicy, stimulating, and serious. The style is unique. The story is purely based on the "smuggling" issue in North China. The content focuses on national survival and movement. It is an excellent reference material for those who study "smuggling issues." The book is a 16-open format, with dozens of pictures planned, plus straightforward, short text explanations, and a color cover. It is also heard that the book has been fully printed and is priced at only 15 cents of national currency. It is published by the Popular Books Publishing House and distributed by major magazine companies and news vendors.
